So I said to him: "In which of this do I need to consult my parents? I want God and His Messenger and the Final Abode."

It was likewise related in mu'allaq (suspended) form from al-Layth: Yunus narrated to me, from al-Zuhri, from Abu Salamah, from A'ishah, who mentioned it, adding: She said: Then the wives of the Prophet ﷺ did just as I had done.

Al-Bukhari related that Ma'mar was inconsistent, sometimes relating it from al-Zuhri from Abu Salamah, and sometimes relating it from al-Zuhri from Urwah from A'ishah.

Ibn Jarir said: Ahmad ibn Abdah al-Dabbi narrated to us, Abu Awanah narrated to us, from Umar ibn Abi Salamah, from his father, who said: A'ishah said: When the verse of choice was revealed, the Messenger of God ﷺ said to me: "I want to mention something to you, but do not decide anything about it until you consult your parents." She said: I said: "And what is it, O Messenger of God?" She said: He put it off from her. So she said: "What is it, O Messenger of God?" She said: He recited to her: {O Prophet, say to your wives, if you desire the life of this world and its adornment} to the end of the verse. She said: I said: "Rather, we choose God and His Messenger and the Final Abode." She said: The Prophet ﷺ was pleased with that.

Ibn Waki' narrated to us, Muhammad ibn Bishr narrated to us, from Muhammad ibn Amr, from Abu Salamah, from A'ishah, may God be pleased with her, who said: When the verse of the choice was revealed, the Messenger of God ﷺ began with me, and said: "O A'ishah, I am presenting to you a matter, but do not give me your answer about it until you present it to your parents, Abu Bakr and Umm Ruman." I said: "O Messenger of God, what is it?" He said: "God, mighty and glorious, has said: {O Prophet, say to your wives, if you desire the life of this world and its adornment, then come, I will provide for you and release you with a gracious release. But if you desire God and His Messenger and the Final Abode, then indeed God has prepared for the doers of good among you a great reward}." She said: "I want God and His Messenger and the Final Abode, and I will not consult my parents, Abu Bakr and Umm Ruman, about that." The Messenger of God ﷺ laughed, then went around to the chambers and said: "A'ishah said such and such." So they said: "We say the same as A'ishah said," may God be pleased with all of them.

Ibn Abi Hatim related it from Abu Sa'id al-Ashajj, from Abu Usamah, from Muhammad ibn Amr, with it.

Ibn Jarir said: Sa'id ibn Yahya al-Umawi narrated to us, my father narrated to us, from Muhammad ibn Ishaq, from Abdullah ibn Abi Bakr, from Amrah, from A'ishah: that when the Messenger of God ﷺ came down to his wives, he was commanded to give them the choice. He entered upon me and said: "I am going to mention something to you, but do not hasten until you consult your father." I said: "And what is it, O Prophet of God?" He said: "I have been commanded to give you the choice," and he recited to her the verse of the choice, to the end of the two verses. She said: I said: "What is it that you are saying, that I should not hasten until I consult my father? I choose God and His Messenger." He was pleased with that, and he presented it to his wives, and they followed one after another, all of them choosing God and His Messenger.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Yazid ibn Sinan al-Basri narrated to us, Abu Salih Abdullah ibn Salih narrated to us, al-Layth narrated to me, Uqayl narrated to me, from al-Zuhri, Ubaydullah ibn Abdullah ibn Abi Thawr informed me, from Ibn Abbas, may God be pleased with both of them, who said: A'ishah, may God be pleased with her, said: The verse of the choice was revealed, and he began with me, the first of his wives, and said: "I am going to mention something to you, but you need not hasten before consulting your parents." She said: He knew that my parents would not have commanded me to leave him. She said: Then he said: "God has said: {O Prophet, say to your wives}," the two verses. A'ishah said: I said: "Is it about this that I should consult my parents? I want God and His Messenger and the Final Abode." Then he gave all his wives the choice, and they said the same as A'ishah had said, may God be pleased with them.

Al-Bukhari and Muslim both related it together, from Qutaybah, from al-Layth, from al-Zuhri, from Urwah, from A'ishah, similarly.

The Imam Ahmad said: Abu Mu'awiyah narrated to us, al-A'mash narrated to us, from Muslim ibn Subayh, from Masruq, from A'ishah, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ gave us the choice, and we chose him, and he did not count that as anything against us (i.e., as a divorce). Both [Bukhari and Muslim] related it from the hadith of al-A'mash.

The Imam Ahmad said: Abu Amir Abd al-Malik ibn Amr narrated to us, Zakariyya ibn Ishaq narrated to us, from Abu al-Zubayr, from Jabir, who said: Abu Bakr, may God be pleased with him, came seeking permission to enter upon the Messenger of God ﷺ while people were sitting at his door, and the Prophet ﷺ was sitting. He was not given permission. Then Umar came and sought permission, and he was not given permission. Then Abu Bakr and Umar were given permission and they entered while the Prophet ﷺ was sitting with his wives around him, and he was silent. Umar said: "I will speak to the Prophet ﷺ, perhaps he will laugh." Umar said: "O Messenger of God, if only you had seen the daughter of Zayd, Umar's wife, she just asked me for maintenance, and I struck her on the neck." The Prophet ﷺ laughed until his molars showed, and said: "They are around me asking me for maintenance." Abu Bakr, may God be pleased with him, got up toward A'ishah to strike her, and Umar, may God be pleased with him, got up toward Hafsah, both of them saying: "You ask the Prophet ﷺ for what he does not have." The Messenger of God ﷺ forbade them both. Then his wives said: "By God, we will never again ask the Messenger of God for what he does not have, after this gathering." He said: And God, mighty and glorious, sent down the choice. He began with A'ishah and said: "I am mentioning something to you which I would not like you to hasten about, until you consult your parents." She said: "What is it?" He said: Then he recited to her: {O Prophet, say to your wives}, the verse. A'ishah, may God be pleased with her, said: "Should I consult my parents about you? Rather, I choose God and His Messenger, and I ask you not to mention to any of your other wives what I have chosen." He said: "God Most High did not send me to be harsh, but sent me as a teacher, making things easy. No woman among them will ask me about what you have chosen except that I will tell her."

Muslim related it alone, without al-Bukhari, and he and al-Nasa'i related it from the hadith of Zakariyya ibn Ishaq al-Makki, with it.

Abdullah ibn al-Imam Ahmad said: Surayj ibn Yunus narrated to us, Ali ibn Hashim ibn al-Barid narrated to us, from Muhammad ibn Ubaydullah ibn Ali ibn Abi Rafi', from Uthman ibn Ali ibn al-Husayn, from his father, from Ali, may God be pleased with him: that the Messenger of God ﷺ gave his wives the choice of this world and the Hereafter, and did not give them the choice of divorce.

This is munqati' (a report with a broken chain), and something similar has been related from al-Hasan and Qatadah and others. It goes against the apparent meaning of the verse, for He said: {then come, I will provide for you and release you with a gracious release}, that is: I will give you your due rights and set you free.

The scholars differed over whether it was permissible for someone else to marry them had he divorced them, into two views, the most correct of which is that it would be, if it were to occur, so that the purpose of release would be achieved. And God knows best.

Ikrimah said: He had nine wives at that time, five of them from Quraysh: A'ishah, Hafsah, Umm Habibah, Sawdah, and Umm Salamah. Also his wives ﷺ were Safiyyah bint Huyayy al-Nadariyyah, Maymunah bint al-Harith al-Hilaliyyah, Zaynab bint Jahsh al-Asadiyyah, and Juwayriyyah bint al-Harith al-Mustaliqiyyah, may God be pleased with them and grant them satisfaction.

He did not marry any of them except after Khadijah bint Khuwaylid ibn Asad ibn Abd al-Uzza ibn Qusayy ibn Kilab had died. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ had married her in Mecca when he was twenty-five years old, and she remained with him until Allah honored him with His message, whereupon she believed in him and supported him, and she was for him a true helper (wazir sidq). She died three years before the Hijrah, according to the most correct view, may Allah be pleased with her. She had distinguishing qualities, among them that he did not marry anyone else while she was his wife, that all his children were from her except Ibrahim, who was from his concubine Mariyah, and that she was the best of the women of this nation.

There is disagreement, expressed in three views, over whether she is superior to Aisha, the third view being to withhold judgment.

Our teacher Abu al-Abbas ibn Taymiyyah was asked about the two of them and said: each of them was distinguished by a particular quality. Khadijah's influence was in the earliest period of Islam. She used to console the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, steady him, and calm him, and she spent her wealth in support of him. She witnessed the very first dawn of Islam and bore harm for the sake of Allah and His Messenger, and her support for the Messenger came at the time of greatest need, so she has a share of support and generosity that no one else has. Aisha's influence was in the later period of Islam, so she has a share in understanding of the religion, in conveying it to the nation, and in the benefit her sons (in knowledge) derived from what she transmitted to them, that no one else has. This is the meaning of his words, may Allah be pleased with him.

Among her distinguishing qualities is that Allah, glorified is He, sent greetings of peace to her through Gabriel, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ conveyed that to her. Al-Bukhari related in his Sahih from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: Gabriel (peace be upon him) came to the Prophet ﷺ and said, "O Messenger of Allah, here is Khadijah coming with a vessel containing seasoning, or food, or drink. When she comes to you, convey to her greetings of peace from her Lord and from me, and give her the glad tidings of a house in Paradise made of reeds, in which there is no clamor and no weariness." This, by the life of Allah, is a distinction that belonged to no one but her. As for Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, Gabriel conveyed greetings of peace to her through the tongue of the Prophet ﷺ. Al-Bukhari related with his chain that Aisha said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said one day, "O Aisha, this is Gabriel conveying to you greetings of peace." I said, "And upon him be peace and the mercy of Allah and His blessings, you see what I do not see," meaning the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. Among the distinguishing qualities of Khadijah, may Allah be pleased with her, is that she never once displeased him, never angered him, and he never took an oath of separation (ila') from her, nor did he ever reproach her or withdraw from her. This alone is sufficient as a virtue and merit.

Among her distinguishing qualities is that she was the first woman of this nation to believe in Allah and His Messenger.

Chapter:

When Allah caused her death, he married after her Sawdah bint Zam'ah, may Allah be pleased with her, that is, Sawdah bint Zam'ah ibn Qays ibn Abd Shams ibn Abd Wudd ibn Nasr ibn Malik ibn Jabal ibn Amir ibn Lu'ayy. She grew old in his household, and he intended to divorce her, so she gave up her day to Aisha, and he kept her as his wife. This is among her distinguishing qualities: that she gave preference, out of her love for the Prophet ﷺ, to giving up her day, seeking closeness to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and out of love for him, preferring to preserve her position with him over the day itself. So he would allocate to Aisha both her own day and Sawdah's day, and he would allocate days to his other wives, but not to her, and she was content with that and gave preference to it, in order to please the Messenger of Allah ﷺ.

He married the truthful woman (al-Siddiqah), daughter of the truthful man (al-Siddiq), Aisha bint Abi Bakr, may Allah be pleased with them both, when she was six years old, two years before the Hijrah, and it is also said three years before. He consummated the marriage with her in Medina at the beginning of his arrival there, in the first year, when she was nine years old. He died while she was eighteen years old. She died in Medina and was buried in al-Baqi'. She left instructions that Abu Hurayrah should lead the prayer over her, in the year fifty-eight. Among her distinguishing qualities is that she was the most beloved of the wives of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ to him, as is established from him in al-Bukhari and elsewhere, that he was asked, "Who is the most beloved of people to you?" He said, "Aisha." It was said, "And among men?" He said, "Her father."

Among her distinguishing qualities also is that he married no other virgin besides her. And among her distinguishing qualities is that revelation would come down upon him while he was under her blanket, and not that of any other wife.

Among her distinguishing qualities is that when Allah, mighty and majestic, revealed to him the verse of the choice, He began with her, giving her the choice first, saying: {"And it is not upon you if you do not hasten, until you consult your parents,"} so she said, "Should I consult my parents about this? Indeed I desire Allah and His Messenger and the abode of the Hereafter." So the rest of his wives ﷺ followed her example, and they said as she had said.

Among her distinguishing qualities is that Allah, glorified is He, cleared her of what the people of the slander accused her of, and revealed regarding her innocence and her exoneration a revelation that is recited in the prayer-niches of the Muslims and in their prayers until the Day of Resurrection. He testified for her that she was among the pure ones, and He promised her forgiveness and a generous provision. He, glorified is He, informed that what was said about her by way of slander was in fact good for her, and that what was said about her was neither harm to her, nor a flaw in her, nor a lowering of her standing. Rather, Allah raised her rank through it, elevated her worth, magnified her standing, and made for her a mention of purity and exoneration among the people of the earth and the heavens. What a virtue, how great it is! Consider this honor and favor arising from her extreme humility and her belittling of herself, when she said, "And my own affair in my own eyes was too insignificant for Allah to speak concerning me with a revelation that would be recited. Rather, I had hoped that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ might see a dream through which Allah would clear me." This is the truthful woman of the nation, the mother of the believers, and the beloved of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and she knew that she was innocent and wronged, and that those who slandered her were wrongdoers, fabricators against her, whose harm had reached even her parents and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, yet this was her own belittling of herself and her own diminishing of her standing. What then do you think of one who has fasted a day or two, or a month or two, who has stood in prayer a night or two, and upon whom some spiritual states have appeared, and who then regards himself as deserving of miraculous graces, as one whose meeting is sought for blessing, whose righteous supplication is to be seized upon, whom people are obligated to respect, honor, esteem, and revere, whose garments are to be touched for blessing, whose doorstep dust is to be kissed, and who holds with Allah a station for which He would take vengeance against whoever belittles him at once, and that whoever is discourteous toward him should be seized without delay, and that discourtesy toward him is a sin that nothing atones for except his own approval?

If this were merely a matter of falling short, it would be a lesser thing, but it is rather a matter of being far behind. These follies and rash presumptions are the product of sheer ignorance and a mind that is not upright, for such things arise only from an ignorant person, pleased with himself, heedless of his own crime, his faults, and his sins, deceived by Allah's granting him respite instead of seizing him for the arrogance and contempt he holds toward one who may well be better than him in Allah's sight. We ask Allah for well-being in this world and the next. The servant should seek refuge in Allah from being great in his own eyes while being lowly in the eyes of Allah. Among the distinguishing qualities of Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, is that the senior Companions, may Allah be pleased with them, when a matter of religion was unclear to them, would consult her, and they would find the knowledge of it with her.

Among her distinguishing qualities is that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ died in her house. Among her distinguishing qualities is that the angel showed her likeness to the Prophet ﷺ before he married her, in a piece of silk cloth, and the Prophet ﷺ said, "If this is from Allah, He will bring it to pass." Among her distinguishing qualities is that people used to time their gifts to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ for her day, seeking closeness to the Messenger ﷺ, so they would present him with what he loved in the house of the wife most beloved to him among his wives, may Allah be pleased with all of them. She was known by the honorific Umm Abdullah. It has been related that she miscarried a child by the Prophet ﷺ, but this is not established as reliable.

The Messenger of Allah ﷺ married Hafsah bint Umar ibn al-Khattab. Before him she had been married to Khunays ibn Hudhafah, who was among the Companions of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and among those who were present at Badr. She died in the year seven, or it is also said, twenty-eight. Among her distinguishing qualities is what the Hafiz Abu Muhammad al-Maqdisi mentioned in his abridgment of the Sirah: that the Prophet ﷺ divorced her, then Gabriel came to him and said, "Allah commands you to take Hafsah back, for she fasts much and prays much at night, and she is your wife in Paradise."

Al-Tabarani said in al-Mu'jam al-Kabir: [chain] Ahmad ibn Tahir ibn Harmalah ibn Yahya narrated to us, my grandfather Harmalah narrated to us, Ibn Wahb narrated to us, Amr ibn Salih al-Hadrami narrated to us, from Musa ibn Ali ibn Rabah, from his father, from Uqbah ibn Amir, that the Prophet ﷺ divorced Hafsah. This reached Umar ibn al-Khattab, and he put dust on his head and said: "God will not care about the son of al-Khattab after this." Then Gabriel (peace be upon him) descended upon the Prophet ﷺ and said: "God commands you to take Hafsah back, as a mercy to Umar."

The Messenger of God ﷺ married Umm Habibah, daughter of Abu Sufyan, whose name was Ramlah bint Sakhr ibn Harb ibn Umayyah ibn Abd Shams ibn Abd Manaf. She had migrated with her husband Abdullah ibn Jahsh to the land of Abyssinia, where he converted to Christianity, but God completed her Islam for her. The Messenger of God ﷺ married her while she was in the land of Abyssinia, and gave her a dower of four hundred dinars before the Negus. The Messenger of God ﷺ sent Amr ibn Umayyah al-Damri to bring her from the land of Abyssinia, and he appointed Uthman ibn Affan to conduct her marriage contract, though it is also said that it was Khalid ibn Sa'id ibn al-As. She is the one who honored the Prophet's ﷺ bedding by not letting her father sit on it when Abu Sufyan came to Madinah, saying to him: "You are a polytheist," and preventing him from sitting on it.

The Messenger of God ﷺ married Umm Salamah, whose name was Hind bint Abi Umayyah ibn al-Mughirah ibn Abdullah ibn Amr ibn Makhzum ibn Yaqzah ibn Murrah ibn Ka'b ibn Lu'ayy ibn Ghalib. Before him she had been married to Abu Salamah ibn Abd al-Asad. She died in the year sixty-two and was buried in al-Baqi'. She was the last of the Prophet's ﷺ wives to die, though it is also said that it was rather Maymunah. Among her distinctions was that Gabriel came to the Prophet ﷺ while she was with him, and she saw him in the form of Dihyah al-Kalbi. In Sahih Muslim, from Abu Uthman, who said: "I was informed that Gabriel came to the Prophet ﷺ while Umm Salamah was with him." He said: "He began speaking, then got up, and the Prophet of God ﷺ said to Umm Salamah: 'Who was that?' or words to that effect. She said: 'This is Dihyah al-Kalbi.' She said: 'By God, I thought it was none other than him, until I heard the Prophet's ﷺ sermon informing that it was Gabriel,' or words to that effect." Sulayman al-Taymi said: "I said to Abu Uthman: 'From whom did you hear this hadith?' He said: 'From Usamah ibn Zayd.'" Her son Umar gave her in marriage to the Messenger of God ﷺ. A group rejected this, saying that her son was not, at that time, of an age sufficient to conduct a marriage contract. Imam Ahmad rejected this claim and disapproved of those who said it. What supports the correctness of Ahmad's position is what Muslim related in his Sahih, that Umar ibn Abi Salamah, her son, asked the Prophet ﷺ about kissing while fasting. He said: "Ask this one," meaning Umm Salamah, and she informed him that the Messenger of God ﷺ did this. He said: "We are not like the Messenger of God ﷺ; God permits His Messenger whatever He wills." The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I am the most God-fearing of you toward God and the most knowledgeable of you about Him," or words to that effect. Such a thing would not be said to someone very young, and Umar was born in the land of Abyssinia before the migration. Al-Bayhaqi said: "The claim of those who assert that he was young is a mere assertion, and his youth has not been established by any sound chain of transmission."

The Messenger of God ﷺ married Zaynab bint Jahsh, of Banu Khuzaymah ibn Mudrikah ibn Ilyas ibn Mudar. She was the daughter of his paternal aunt Umaymah bint Abd al-Muttalib. Before him she had been married to his freedman Zayd ibn Harithah, who divorced her, and God married her to him from above seven heavens, and revealed to him: {So when Zayd had accomplished what he willed of her, We married her to you}. So he went in and entered upon her without seeking permission. She used to boast of this over the rest of the Prophet's ﷺ wives, saying: "Your families married you off, but God married me off from above His seven heavens." This was one of her distinctions. She died in Madinah in the year twenty, and was buried in al-Baqi'.

The Prophet ﷺ married Zaynab bint Khuzaymah al-Hilaliyyah, who had been married to Abdullah ibn Jahsh. He married her in the third year of the Hijrah. She was called Umm al-Masakin (Mother of the Poor). She remained with the Messenger of God ﷺ only a short time, two or three months, and then died, may God be pleased with her.

The Messenger of God ﷺ married Juwayriyyah bint al-Harith, of Banu al-Mustaliq. She had been taken captive in the raid against Banu al-Mustaliq, and fell to the lot of Thabit ibn Qays, who made a contract with her for her manumission. The Messenger of God ﷺ paid off her contract and married her in the sixth year of the Hijrah. She died in the year fifty-six. It was on her account that the Muslims freed a hundred households of slaves, saying: "They are the in-laws of the Messenger of God ﷺ." That was part of her blessing upon her people.

The Messenger of God ﷺ married Safiyyah bint Huyayy, a descendant of Aaron ibn Amran, brother of Moses, in the seventh year. She had been taken captive from Khaybar. Before him she had been married to Kinanah ibn Abi al-Huqayq, whom the Messenger of God ﷺ had killed. She died in the year thirty-six, though it is also said in the year fifty. Among her distinctions was that the Messenger of God ﷺ freed her and made her manumission her dower. Anas said: "He gave her herself as her dower," and this became a precedent for the ummah until the Day of Resurrection: it is permissible for a man to make the manumission of his slave woman her dower, and she becomes his wife, according to the explicit statement of Imam Ahmad, may God have mercy on him. Al-Tirmidhi said: [chain] Ishaq ibn Mansur and Abd ibn Humayd narrated to us, they said, Abd al-Razzaq narrated to us, Ma'mar narrated to us, from Thabit, from Anas, who said: "It reached Safiyyah that Hafsah had said: 'Safiyyah, daughter of a Jew.' So she wept. The Prophet ﷺ came in to her while she was weeping and said: 'What makes you weep?' She said: 'Hafsah said to me: I am the daughter of a Jew.' The Prophet ﷺ said: 'You are indeed the daughter of a prophet, and your uncle is indeed a prophet, and you are indeed married to a prophet, so what does she have to boast over you about?' Then he said: 'Fear God, O Hafsah.'" Al-Tirmidhi said: "This is a sound, gharib (singular) hadith from this route." This was one of her distinctions, may God be pleased with her.

The Messenger of God ﷺ married Maymunah bint al-Harith al-Hilaliyyah. He married her at Saraf, which is nine miles from Makkah. She was the last of the Mothers of the Believers whom he married. She died in the year sixty-three. She was the maternal aunt of Khalid ibn al-Walid and of Ibn Abbas, for his mother was Umm al-Fadl bint al-Harith. There is disagreement over the Prophet's ﷺ marriage to her: whether he married her in a state of ihram or not. The correct view is that he married her while not in a state of ihram, as Abu Rafi' al-Shafir stated regarding her marriage.

The hafiz Abu Muhammad al-Maqdisi and others said: "He contracted marriage with seven women whom he did not consummate the marriage with." The prayer upon his wives follows from the respect due to them and their being forbidden to the ummah, and from the fact that they are his ﷺ wives in this world and the next. As for any woman he separated from during her lifetime without consummating the marriage, the rulings pertaining to his wives whom he did consummate marriage with do not apply to her. May God's peace and blessings be upon him, and upon his wives, his family, and his descendants, abundantly.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا أَمْرٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ لِرَسُولِهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ ، بِأَنْ يخَيّر نِسَاءَهُ بَيْنَ أَنْ يُفَارِقَهُنَّ، فَيَذْهَبْنَ إِلَى غَيْرِهِ مِمَّنْ يَحصُل لَهُنَّ عِنْدَهُ الحياةُ الدُّنْيَا وَزِينَتُهَا، وَبَيْنَ الصَّبْرِ عَلَى مَا عِنْدَهُ مِنْ ضِيقِ الْحَالِ، وَلَهُنَّ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ فِي ذَلِكَ الثَّوَابُ الْجَزِيلُ، فَاخْتَرْنَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُنَّ وَأَرْضَاهُنَّ، اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالدَّارَ الْآخِرَةَ، فَجَمَعَ اللَّهُ لَهُنَّ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ بَيْنَ خَيْرِ الدُّنْيَا وَسَعَادَةِ الْآخِرَةِ.

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْيَمَانِ، أَخْبَرَنَا شُعَيْبٌ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، قَالَ: أَخْبَرَنِي أَبُو سَلَمَةَ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، أَنَّ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، زَوْجَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَخْبَرَتْهُ: أن رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم جَاءَهَا حِينَ أَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُخَيِّرَ أَزْوَاجَهُ، فَبَدَأَ بِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ: "إِنِّي ذَاكِرٌ لَكِ أَمْرًا، فَلَا عَلَيْكِ أَنْ لَا تَسْتَعْجِلِي حَتَّى تَسْتَأْمِرِي أَبَوَيْكِ"، وَقَدْ عَلمَ أَنَّ أَبَوَيَّ لَمْ يَكُونَا يَأْمُرَانِي بِفِرَاقِهِ. قَالَتْ: ثُمَّ قَالَ: "وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ قَالَ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ قُلْ لِأَزْوَاجِكَ﴾ إِلَى تَمَامِ الْآيَتَيْنِ، فَقُلْتُ لَهُ: فَفِي أَيِّ هَذَا أَسْتَأْمِرُ أَبَوَيَّ؟ فَإِنِّي أُرِيدُ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالدَّارَ الْآخِرَةَ .

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ مُعَلَّقًا عَنِ اللَّيْثِ: حَدَّثَنِي يُونُسُ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، فَذَكَرَهُ وَزَادَ: قَالَتْ: ثُمَّ فَعَلَ أَزْوَاجُ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ مِثْلَ مَا فَعَلْتُ .

وَقَدْ حَكَى الْبُخَارِيُّ أَنَّ مَعْمَرًا اضْطَرَبَ، فَتَارَةً رَوَاهُ عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، وَتَارَةً رَوَاهُ عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُرْوَة، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عبَدة الضَّبِّي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَوَانة، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: لَمَّا نَزَلَ الْخِيَارُ قَالَ لِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنِّي أُرِيدُ أَنْ أَذْكُرَ لَكِ أَمْرًا، فَلَا تَقْضِي فِيهِ شَيْئًا حَتَّى تَسْتَأْمِرِي أَبَوَيْكِ". قَالَتْ: قُلْتُ: وَمَا هُوَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: فَرَدَّهُ عَلَيْهَا. فَقَالَتْ: فَمَا هُوَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَتْ: فَقَرَأَ عَلَيْهَا: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ قُلْ لأزْوَاجِكَ إِنْ كُنْتُنَّ تُرِدْنَ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا وَزِينَتَهَا﴾ إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَةِ. قَالَتْ: فَقُلْتُ: بَلْ نَخْتَارُ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالدَّارَ الْآخِرَةَ. قَالَتْ: فَفَرِحَ بِذَلِكَ النَّبِيُّ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم وَحَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بِشْرٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ آيَةُ التَّخْيِيرِ، بَدَأَ بِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ: "يَا عَائِشَةُ، إني عارض عليك أمرًا، فلا تُفتياني فِيهِ [بِشَيْءٍ] حَتَّى تَعْرِضِيهِ عَلَى أَبَوَيْكِ أَبِي بَكْرٍ وَأُمِّ رُومَانَ". فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، وَمَا هُوَ؟ قَالَ: "قَالَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ قُلْ لأزْوَاجِكَ إِنْ كُنْتُنَّ تُرِدْنَ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا وَزِينَتَهَا فَتَعَالَيْنَ أُمَتِّعْكُنَّ وَأُسَرِّحْكُنَّ سَرَاحًا جَمِيلا. وَإِنْ كُنْتُنَّ تُرِدْنَ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالدَّارَ الآخِرَةَ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ أَعَدَّ لِلْمُحْسِنَاتِ مِنْكُنَّ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا﴾ .قَالَتْ: فَإِنِّي أُرِيدُ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالدَّارَ الْآخِرَةَ، وَلَا أُؤَامِرُ فِي ذَلِكَ أَبَوَيَّ أَبَا بَكْرٍ وَأُمَّ رُومَانَ، فَضَحِكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، ثُمَّ اسْتَقْرَأَ الحُجَر فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ عَائِشَةَ قَالَتْ كَذَا وَكَذَا". فَقُلْنَ: وَنَحْنُ نَقُولُ مِثْلَ مَا قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُنَّ كُلِّهِنَّ .

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الأشَجِّ، عَنْ أَبِي أُسَامَةَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، بِهِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَحَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ يَحْيَى الْأُمَوِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، عَنْ عَمرة، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَمَّا نَزَلَ إِلَى نِسَائِهِ أُمِرَ أَنْ يُخَيِّرَهُنَّ، فَدَخَلَ عَليَّ فَقَالَ: "سَأَذْكُرُ لَكِ أَمْرًا فَلَا تَعْجَلِي حَتَّى تَسْتَشِيرِي أَبَاكِ". فَقُلْتُ: وَمَا هُوَ يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "إِنِّي أُمِرْتُ أَنْ أُخَيِّرَكُنَّ"، وَتَلَا عَلَيْهَا آيَةَ التَّخْيِيرِ، إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَتَيْنِ. قَالَتْ: فَقُلْتُ: وَمَا الَّذِي تَقُولُ لَا تَعْجَلِي حَتَّى تَسْتَشِيرِي أَبَاكِ؟ فَإِنِّي اخْتَارُ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ، فَسُرّ بِذَلِكَ، وعَرَض عَلَى نِسَائِهِ فَتَتَابَعْنَ كُلّهن، فاخترنَ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ سِنَانٍ الْبَصْرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو صَالِحٍ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ صَالِحٍ، حَدَّثَنِي اللَّيْثُ، حَدَّثَنِي عُقَيل، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيُّ، أخبرنَي عُبيد اللَّهِ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي ثَور، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، قَالَ: قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا: أُنْزِلَتْ آيَةُ التَّخْيِيرِ فَبَدَأَ بِي أَوَّلَ امْرَأَةٍ مِنْ نِسَائِهِ، فَقَالَ: "إِنِّي ذَاكِرٌ لَكِ أَمْرًا، فَلَا عَلَيْكِ أَلَّا تَعْجَلِي حَتَّى تَسْتَأْمِرِي أَبَوَيْكِ". قَالَتْ: قَدْ عَلِم أَنَّ أَبَوَيَّ لَمْ يَكُونَا يَأْمُرَانِي بِفِرَاقِهِ. قَالَتْ: ثُمَّ قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَالَ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ قُلْ لأزْوَاجِكَ﴾ الْآيَتَيْنِ. قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: فَقُلْتُ: أَفِي هَذَا أَسْتَأْمِرُ أَبَوَيَّ؟ فَإِنِّي أُرِيدُ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالدَّارَ الْآخِرَةَ. ثُمَّ خَيَّرَ نِسَاءَهُ كُلَّهُنَّ، فَقُلْنَ مِثْلَ مَا قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُنَّ.

وَأَخْرَجَهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ وَمُسْلِمٌ جَمِيعًا، عَنْ قُتَيْبَةَ، عَنِ اللَّيْثِ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ مِثْلَهُ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ مُسْلِمِ بْنِ صَبِِيح، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ قَالَتْ: خَيَّرَنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَاخْتَرْنَاهُ، فَلَمْ يَعُدَّهَا عَلَيْنَا شَيْئًا. أَخْرَجَاهُ مِنْ حديث الأعمش وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَامِرٍ عَبْدُ الْمَلِكِ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، حَدَّثَنَا زَكَرِيَّا بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ أَبِي الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: أَقْبَلَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، يَسْتَأْذِنُ عَلَى رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم والناس بِبَابِهِ جُلُوسٌ، وَالنَّبِيُّ ﷺ جَالِسٌ: فَلَمْ يُؤْذَنْ لَهُ. ثُمَّ أَقْبَلَ عُمَرُ فَاسْتَأْذَنَ فَلَمْ يُؤْذَنْ لَهُ. ثُمَّ أَذِنَ لِأَبِي بَكْرٍ وَعُمَرَ فَدَخْلَا وَالنَّبِيُّ ﷺ جَالِسٌ وَحَوْلَهُ نِسَاؤُهُ، وَهُوَ سَاكِتٌ، فَقَالَ عُمَرُ: لَأُكَلِّمَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ لَعَلَّهُ يَضْحَكُ، فَقَالَ عُمَرُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، لَوْ رَأَيْتَ ابْنَةَ زَيْدٍ -امْرَأَةَ عُمَرَ -سَأَلَتْنِي النَّفَقَةَ آنِفًا، فَوَجَأْتُ عُنُقَهَا. فَضَحِكَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ حَتَّى بَدَا نَاجِذُهُ وَقَالَ: "هُنَّ حَوْلِي يَسْأَلْنَنِي النَّفَقَةَ". فَقَامَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، إِلَى عَائِشَةَ لِيَضْرِبَهَا، وَقَامَ عُمَرُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، إِلَى حَفْصَةَ، كِلَاهُمَا يَقُولَانِ: تَسْأَلَانِ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ مَا لَيْسَ عِنْدَهُ. فَنَهَاهُمَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقُلْنَ نِسَاؤُهُ: وَاللَّهِ لَا نَسْأَلُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ بَعْدَ هَذَا الْمَجْلِسِ مَا لَيْسَ عِنْدَهُ. قَالَ: وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، الْخِيَارَ، فَبَدَأَ بِعَائِشَةَ فَقَالَ: "إِنِّي أَذْكُرُ لَكِ أَمْرًا مَا أُحِبُّ أَنْ تَعْجَلِي فِيهِ حَتَّى تَسْتَأْمِرِي أَبَوَيْكِ". قَالَتْ: وَمَا هُوَ؟ قَالَ: فَتَلَا عَلَيْهَا: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ قُلْ لأزْوَاجِكَ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا: أَفِيكَ أَسْتَأْمِرُ أَبَوَيَّ؟ بَلْ أَخْتَارُ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ، وَأَسْأَلُكَ أَلَّا تَذْكُرَ لِامْرَأَةٍ مِنْ نِسَائِكَ مَا اخْتَرْتُ. فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى لَمْ يَبْعَثْنِي مُعَنِّفًا، وَلَكِنْ بَعَثَنِي مُعَلِّمًا مُيَسِّرًا ، لَا تَسْأَلَنِي امْرَأَةٌ مِنْهُنَّ عَمَّا اخترتِ إِلَّا أخبرتُها".

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ مُسْلِمٌ دُونَ الْبُخَارِيِّ، فَرَوَاهُ هُوَ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ زَكَرِيَّا بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ الْمَكِّيِّ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُرَيْج بْنُ يُونُسَ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ هَاشِمِ بْنِ الْبَرِيدِ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عُبَيْدِ [اللَّهِ بْنِ عَلِيِّ] بْنِ أَبِي رَافِعٍ، عَنْ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ خَيَّر نِسَاءَهُ الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةَ، وَلَمْ يُخَيِّرْهُنَّ الطَّلَاقَ .

وَهَذَا مُنْقَطِعٌ، وَقَدْ رُوي عَنِ الْحَسَنِ وَقَتَادَةَ وَغَيْرِهِمَا نَحْوُ ذَلِكَ. وَهُوَ خِلَافُ الظَّاهِرِ مِنَ الْآيَةِ، فَإِنَّهُ قَالَ: ﴿فَتَعَالَيْنَ أُمَتِّعْكُنَّ وَأُسَرِّحْكُنَّ سَرَاحًا جَمِيلا﴾ أي: أعطيكن حُقُوقَكُنَّ وَأُطْلِقْ سَرَاحَكُنَّ.

وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفَ الْعُلَمَاءُ فِي جَوَازِ تَزْوِيجِ غَيْرِهِ لَهُنَّ لَوْ طَلَّقَهُنَّ، عَلَى قَوْلَيْنِ، وَأَصَحُّهُمَا نَعَمْ لَوْ وَقَعَ، لِيَحْصُلَ الْمَقْصُودُ مِنَ السَّرَاحِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: وَكَانَ تَحْتَهُ يَوْمَئِذٍ تِسْعُ نِسْوَةٍ، خَمْسٌ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ: عَائِشَةُ، وَحَفْصَةُ، وَأُمُّ حَبِيبَةَ، وَسَوْدَةُ، وَأُمُّ سَلَمَةَ، وَكَانَتْ تَحْتَهُ ﷺ صَفِيَّةُ بِنْتُ حُيَيّ النَّضَريَّة، وَمَيْمُونَةُ بِنْتُ الْحَارِثِ الْهِلَالِيَّةُ، وَزَيْنَبُ بِنْتُ جَحْشٍ الْأَسَدِيَّةُ، وَجُوَيْرِيَةُ بِنْتُ الْحَارِثِ الْمُصْطَلِقِيَّةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُنَّ وَأَرْضَاهُنَّ.

[وَلَمْ يَتَزَوَّجْ وَاحِدَةً مِنْهُنَّ، إِلَّا بَعْدَ أَنْ تُوُفِّيَتْ خَدِيجَةُ بِنْتُ خُوَيْلِدِ بْنِ أَسَدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْعُزَّى بْنِ قُصَيِّ بْنِ كِلَابٍ، تَزَوَّجَهَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِمَكَّةَ، وَهُوَ ابْنُ خَمْسٍ وَعِشْرِينَ سَنَةً، وَبَقِيَتْ مَعَهُ إِلَى أَنْ أَكْرَمَهُ اللَّهُ بِرِسَالَتِهِ فَآمَنَتْ بِهِ وَنَصَرَتْهُ، وَكَانَتْ لَهُ وَزِيرَ صِدْقٍ، وَمَاتَتْ قَبْلَ الْهِجْرَةِ بِثَلَاثِ سِنِينَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، فِي الْأَصَحِّ، وَلَهَا خَصَائِصُ مِنْهَا: أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَتَزَوَّجْ عَلَيْهَا غَيْرَهَا، وَمِنْهَا أَنَّ أَوْلَادَهُ كُلَّهُمْ مِنْهَا، إِلَّا إِبْرَاهِيمَ، فَإِنَّهُ مِنْ سُرِّيَّتِهِ مَارِيَةَ، وَمِنْهَا أَنَّهَا خَيْرُ نساء الأمة.

وَاخْتُلِفَ فِي تَفْضِيلِهَا عَلَى عَائِشَةَ عَلَى ثَلَاثَةِ أَقْوَالٍ، ثَالِثُهَا الْوَقْفُ.

وَسُئِلَ شَيْخُنَا أَبُو الْعَبَّاسِ بْنُ تَيْمِيَّةَ عَنْهُمَا فَقَالَ: اخْتُصَّتْ كُلُّ وَاحِدَةٍ مِنْهُمَا بِخَاصِّيَّةٍ، فَخَدِيجَةُ كَانَ تَأْثِيرُهَا فِي أَوَّلِ الْإِسْلَامِ، وَكَانَتْ تُسلِّي رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَتُثَبِّتُهُ، وَتُسَكِّنُهُ، وَتَبْذُلُ دُونَهُ مَالَهَا، فَأَدْرَكَتْ غُرة الْإِسْلَامِ، وَاحْتَمَلَتِ الْأَذَى فِي اللَّهِ وَفِي رَسُولِهِ وَكَانَ نُصْرَتُهَا لِلرَّسُولِ فِي أَعْظَمِ أَوْقَاتِ الْحَاجَةِ، فَلَهَا مِنَ النُّصْرَةِ وَالْبَذْلِ مَا لَيْسَ لِغَيْرِهَا. وَعَائِشَةُ تَأْثِيرُهَا فِي آخِرِ الْإِسْلَامِ، فَلَهَا مِنَ التَّفَقُّهِ فِي الدِّينِ وَتَبْلِيغِهِ إِلَى الْأُمَّةِ، وَانْتِفَاعِ بَنِيهَا بِمَا أدَّت إِلَيْهِمْ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ، مَا لَيْسَ لِغَيْرِهَا. هَذَا مَعْنَى كَلَامِهِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ.

وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أَنَّ اللَّهَ، سُبْحَانَهُ، بَعَثَ إِلَيْهَا السَّلَامَ مَعَ جِبْرِيلَ، فَبَلَّغَهَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ ذَلِكَ. رَوَى الْبُخَارِيُّ فِي صَحِيحِهِ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: أَتَى جِبْرِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، النَّبِيَّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، هَذِهِ خَدِيجَةُ، قَدْ أَتَتْ مَعَهَا إِنَاءٌ فِيهِ إِدَامٌ أَوْ طَعَامٌ أَوْ شراب، فإذا هي أتتك فأقرأها السَّلَامَ مِنْ رَبِّهَا وَمِنِّي، وَبَشِّرْهَا بِبَيْتٍ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، مِنْ قَصَب، لَا صَخَب فِيهِ وَلَا نَصَب وَهَذِهِ لعَمْر اللَّهِ خَاصَّةٌ، لَمْ تَكُنْ لِسِوَاهَا. وَأَمَّا عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، فَإِنَّ جِبْرِيلَ سلَّم عَلَيْهَا عَلَى لِسَانِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَرَوَى الْبُخَارِيُّ بِإِسْنَادِهِ أَنَّ عَائِشَةَ قَالَتْ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَوْمًا: "يَا عَائِشَةُ، هَذَا جِبْرِيلُ يُقْرِئُكِ السَّلَامَ". فَقُلْتُ: وَعَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ وَرَحْمَةُ اللَّهِ وَبَرَكَاتُهُ، تَرَى مَا لَا أَرَى، تُرِيدُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ . وَمَنْ خَوَاصِّ خديجة، رضي الله عنها: أنه لم تسوءه قَطُّ، وَلَمْ تُغَاضِبْهُ، وَلَمْ يَنَلْهَا مِنْهُ إِيلَاءٌ، وَلَا عُتْبٌ قَطُّ، وَلَا هَجْرٌ، وَكَفَى بِهَذِهِ مَنْقَبَةٌ وَفَضِيلَةٌ.

وَمِنْ خَوَاصِّهَا: أَنَّهَا أَوَّلُ امْرَأَةٍ آمَنَتْ بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ.

فَصْلٌ:

فلمَّا تَوَفَّاهَا اللَّهُ تَزَوَّجَ بَعْدَهَا سَوْدَةَ بِنْتَ زَمْعَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، وَهِيَ سَوْدَةُ بِنْتُ زَمْعَةَ بْنِ قَيْسِ بْنِ عَبْدِ شَمْسِ بْنِ عَبْدِ وُدِّ بْنِ نَصْرِ بْنِ مَالِكِ بْنِ جَبَلِ بْنِ عَامِرِ بْنِ لُؤَيٍّ، وَكَبُرَتْ عِنْدَهُ، وَأَرَادَ طَلَاقَهَا فَوَهَبَتْ يَوْمَهَا لِعَائِشَةَ، فَأَمْسَكَهَا. وَهَذَا مِنْ خَوَاصِّهَا: أَنَّهَا آثَرَتْ بِيَوْمِهَا حُبَّ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ تَقَرُّبًا إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَحُبًّا لَهُ، وَإِيثَارًا لِمَقَامِهَا مَعَهُ، فَكَانَ يَقْسِمُ لِعَائِشَةَ يَوْمَهَا وَيَوْمَ سَوْدَةَ، وَيَقْسِمُ لِنِسَائِهِ، وَلَا يَقْسِمُ لَهَا وَهِيَ رَاضِيَةٌ بِذَلِكَ مُؤْثِرَةٌ، لِتُرْضِيَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ.

وَتَزَوَّجَ الصِّدِّيقَةَ بِنْتَ الصِّدِّيقِ عَائِشَةَ بِنْتَ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، وَهِيَ بِنْتُ سِتِّ سِنِينَ قَبْلَ الْهِجْرَةِ بِسَنَتَيْنِ، وَقِيلَ: بِثَلَاثٍ، وَبَنَى بِهَا بِالْمَدِينَةِ أَوَّلَ مَقْدَمِهِ فِي السَّنَةِ الْأُولَى، وَهِيَ بِنْتُ تِسْعٍ، وَمَاتَ عَنْهَا وَهِيَ بِنْتُ ثَمَانِ عَشْرَةَ، وَتُوُفِّيَتْ بِالْمَدِينَةِ، وَدُفِنَتْ بِالْبَقِيعِ، وَأَوْصَتْ أَنْ يُصَلِّيَ عَلَيْهَا أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ سَنَةَ ثَمَانٍ وَخَمْسِينَ، وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أَنَّهَا كَانَتْ أَحَبَّ أَزْوَاجِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِلَيْهِ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ ذَلِكَ عَنْهُ فِي الْبُخَارِيِّ وَغَيْرِهِ، أَنَّهُ سُئِلَ أَيُّ النَّاسِ أَحَبُّ إِلَيْكَ؟ قَالَ: "عَائِشَةُ". قِيلَ: فَمِنَ الرِّجَالِ؟ قَالَ: "أَبُوهَا" .

وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا أَيْضًا: أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَتَزَوَّجْ بِكْرًا غَيْرَهَا، وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أَنَّهُ كان ينزل عليه الوحي وهو فِي لِحَافِهَا دُونَ غَيْرِهَا.

وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أَنَّ اللَّهَ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، لَمَّا أَنْزَلَ عَلَيْهِ آيَةَ التَّخْيِيرِ بَدَأَ بِهَا فَخَيَّرَهَا، فَقَالَ: "وَلَا عَلَيْكِ أَلَّا تَعْجَلِي حَتَّى تَسْتَأْمِرِي أَبَوَيْكِ". فَقَالَتْ: أَفِي هَذَا أَسْتَأْمِرُ أبويَّ، فَإِنِّي أُرِيدُ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالدَّارَ الْآخِرَةَ. فَاسْتَنَّ بِهَا بَقِيَّةُ أَزْوَاجِهِ ﷺ، وَقُلْنَ كَمَا قَالَتْ.

وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أَنَّ اللَّهَ، سُبْحَانَهُ، بَرَّأَهَا مِمَّا رَمَاهَا بِهِ أَهْلُ الْإِفْكِ، وَأَنْزَلَ فِي عُذْرِهَا، وَبَرَاءَتِهَا، وَحْيًا يُتْلَى فِي مَحَارِيبِ الْمُسْلِمِينَ، وَصَلَوَاتِهِمْ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَشَهِدَ لَهَا أَنَّهَا مِنَ الطَّيِّبَاتِ، وَوَعَدَهَا الْمَغْفِرَةَ وَالرِّزْقَ الْكَرِيمَ، وَأَخْبَرَ سُبْحَانَهُ، أَنَّ مَا قِيلَ فِيهَا مِنَ الْإِفْكِ كَانَ خَيْرًا لَهَا، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ بِذَلِكَ الَّذِي قِيلَ فِيهَا شَرٌّ لَهَا، وَلَا عَيْبٌ لَهَا، وَلَا خَافِضٌ مِنْ شَأْنِهَا، بَلْ رَفَعَهَا اللَّهُ بِذَلِكَ، وَأَعْلَى قَدْرَهَا وَعَظَّمَ شَأْنَهَا، وَأَصَارَ لَهَا ذِكْرًا بِالطِّيبِ وَالْبَرَاءَةِ بَيْنَ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ وَالسَّمَاءِ، فَيَا لَهَا مِنْ مَنْقَبَةٍ مَا أَجَلَّهَا. وَتَأَمَّلْ هَذَا التَّشْرِيفَ وَالْإِكْرَامَ النَّاشِئَ عَنْ فَرْطِ تَوَاضُعِهَا وَاسْتِصْغَارِهَا لِنَفْسِهَا، حَيْثُ قَالَتْ: وَلِشَأْنِي فِي نَفْسِي كَانَ أَحْقَرَ مِنْ أَنْ يَتَكَلَّمَ اللَّهُ فيَّ بِوَحْيٍ يُتْلَى، وَلَكِنْ كُنْتُ أَرْجُو أَنْ يَرَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ رُؤْيَا يُبَرِّئُنِي اللَّهُ بِهَا، فَهَذِهِ صِّدِّيقَةُ الْأُمَّةِ، وَأُمُّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَحِبُّ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَهِيَ تَعْلَمُ أَنَّهَا بَرِيئَةٌ مَظْلُومَةٌ، وَأَنَّ قَاذِفِيهَا ظَالِمُونَ مُفْتَرُونَ عَلَيْهَا، قَدْ بَلَغَ أَذَاهُمْ إِلَى أَبَوَيْهَا، وَإِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَهَذَا كَانَ احْتِقَارَهَا لِنَفْسِهَا وَتَصْغِيرَهَا لِشَأْنِهَا، فَمَا ظَنُّكَ بِمَنْ قَدْ صَامَ يَوْمًا أَوْ يَوْمَيْنِ، أَوْ شَهْرًا أَوْ شَهْرَيْنِ، قَدْ قَامَ لَيْلَةً أَوْ لَيْلَتَيْنِ، فَظَهَرَ عَلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ مِنَ الْأَحْوَالِ، وَلَاحَظُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ بِعَيْنِ اسْتِحْقَاقِ الْكَرَامَاتِ، وَأَنَّهُمْ مِمَّنْ يُتَبَرَّكُ بِلِقَائِهِمْ، ويُغتنم بِصَالِحِ دُعَائِهِمْ، وَأَنَّهُمْ يَجِبُ عَلَى النَّاسِ احْتِرَامُهُمْ وَتَعْظِيمُهُمْ وَتَعْزِيزُهُمْ وَتَوْقِيرُهُمْ، فَيُتَمَسَّحُ بِأَثْوَابِهِمْ، وَيُقَبَّلُ ثَرَى أَعِتَابِهِمْ، وَأَنَّهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ بِالْمَكَانَةِ الَّتِي تَنْتَقِمُ لَهُمْ لِأَجْلِهَا مَنْ تَنَقَّصَهَمْ فِي الْحَالِ، وَأَنْ يُؤْخَذَ مَنْ أَسَاءَ الْأَدَبَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ غَيْرِ إِمْهَالٍ، وَإِنَّ إِسَاءَةَ الْأَدَبِ عَلَيْهِمْ ذَنْبٌ لَا يُكَفِّرُهُ شَيْءٌ إِلَّا رِضَاهُمْ.

وَلَوْ كَانَ هَذَا مِنْ وَرَاءِ كِفَايَةٍ لَهَانَ، وَلَكِنَّ مِنْ وَرَاءِ تَخَلُّفٍ، وَهَذِهِ الْحَمَاقَاتُ وَالرُّعُونَاتُ نِتَاجُ الْجَهْلِ الصَّمِيمِ، وَالْعَقْلِ غَيْرِ الْمُسْتَقِيمِ، فَإِنَّ ذَلِكَ إِنَّمَا يَصْدُرُ مِنْ جَاهِلٍ مُعْجَبٍ بِنَفْسِهِ، غَافِلٍ عَنْ جُرْمِهِ وَعُيُوبِهِ وَذُنُوبِهِ، مُغْتَرٍّ بِإِمْهَالِ اللَّهِ لَهُ عَنْ أَخْذِهِ بِمَا هُوَ فِيهِ مِنَ الْكِبْرِ وَالِازْدِرَاءِ عَلَى مَنْ لَعَلَّهُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ خَيْرٌ مِنْهُ. نَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ الْعَافِيَةَ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ. وَيَنْبَغِي لِلْعَبْدِ أَنْ يَسْتَعِيذَ بِاللَّهِ أَنْ يَكُونَ عِنْدَ نَفْسِهِ عَظِيمًا، وَهُوَ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ حَقِيرٌ، وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا: أَنَّ الْأَكَابِرَ مِنَ الصَّحَابَةِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ، كَانَ إِذَا أَشْكَلَ الْأَمْرُ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنَ الدِّينِ، اسْتَفْتَوْهَا فَيَجِدُونَ عِلْمَهُ عِنْدَهَا.

وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أن رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم تُوُفِّيَ فِي بَيْتِهَا. وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أَنَّ الْمَلَكَ أَرَى صُورَتَهَا لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَتَزَوَّجَهَا فِي خِرْقَةِ حَرِيرٍ، فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "إِنَّ يَكُنْ هَذَا مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ يُمْضِهِ" . وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أَنَّ النَّاسَ كَانُوا يَتَحَرَّوْنَ هَدَايَاهُمْ يَوْمَهَا مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ تَقَرُّبًا إِلَى الرَّسُولِ ﷺ، فَيُتْحِفُونَهُ بِمَا يُحِبُّ فِي مَنْزِلِ أَحَبِّ نِسَائِهِ إِلَيْهِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ، وَتُكَنَّى أُمَّ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، وَرُوِيَ أَنَّهَا أَسْقَطَتْ مِنَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ سَقْطًا، وَلَا يَثْبُتْ ذَلِكَ.

وَتَزَوَّجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَفْصَةَ بِنْتَ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، وَكَانَتْ قَبْلَهُ عِنْدَ حُبَيْشِ بْنِ حُذَافَةَ، وَكَانَ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَمِمَّنْ شَهِدَ بَدْرًا، تُوُفِّيَتْ سَنَةَ سَبْعٍ، وَقِيلَ: ثَمَانٍ وَعِشْرِينَ، وَمِنْ خَوَاصِّهَا: مَا ذَكَرَهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو مُحَمَّدٍ الْمَقْدِسِيُّ فِي مُخْتَصَرِهِ فِي السِّيرَةِ: أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ طَلَّقَهَا، فَأَتَاهُ جِبْرِيلُ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَأْمُرُكَ أَنْ تُرَاجِعَ حَفْصَةَ، فَإِنَّهَا صَوَّامَةٌ قَوَّامَةٌ وَإِنَّهَا زَوْجَتُكَ فِي الْجَنَّةِ.

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ فِي الْمُعْجَمِ الْكَبِيرِ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ طَاهِرِ بْنِ حَرْمَلَةَ بْنِ يَحْيَى، حَدَّثَنَا جَدِّي حَرْمَلَةُ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ صَالِحٍ الْحَضْرَمِيُّ، عَنْ مُوسَى بْنِ عَلِيِّ بْنِ رَبَاحٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عُقْبَةَ بْنِ عَامِرٍ، أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ طَلَّقَ حَفْصَةَ، فَبَلَغَ ذَلِكَ عُمَرَ بْنَ الْخَطَّابِ، فَوَضَعَ التُّرَابَ عَلَى رَأْسِهِ، وَقَالَ: مَا يَعْبَأُ اللَّهُ بِابْنِ الْخَطَّابِ بَعْدَ هَذَا. فَنَزَلَ جِبْرِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَأْمُرُكَ أَنْ تُرَاجِعَ حَفْصَةَ رَحْمَةً لِعُمَرَ. 

وَتَزَوَّجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ أُمُّ حَبِيبَةَ بِنْتَ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ، وَاسْمُهَا رَمْلَةُ بِنْتُ صَخْرِ بْنِ حَرْبِ بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ شَمْسِ بْنِ عَبْدِ مَنَافٍ، هَاجَرَتْ مَعَ زَوْجِهَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ جَحْشٍ إِلَى أَرْضِ الْحَبَشَةِ، فَتَنَصَّرَ بِالْحَبَشَةِ، وَأَتَمَّ اللَّهُ لَهَا الْإِسْلَامَ، وَتَزَوَّجَهَا رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهِيَ بِأَرْضِ الْحَبَشَةِ، وَأَصْدَقَهَا عِنْدَ النَّجَاشِيِّ أَرْبَعَمِائَةِ دِينَارٍ، وَبَعَثَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَمْرُو بْنَ أُمَيَّةَ الضَّمْرِيَّ بِهَا إِلَى أَرْضِ الْحَبَشَةِ، وَوَلَّى نِكَاحَهَا عُثْمَانَ بْنَ عَفَّانَ، وَقِيلَ: خَالِدَ بْنَ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْعَاصِ، وَهِيَ الَّتِي أَكْرَمَتْ فِرَاشِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ إن يَجْلِسَ عَلَيْهِ أَبُوهَا لَمَّا قَدِمَ أَبُو سُفْيَانَ الْمَدِينَةَ، وَقَالَتْ لَهُ: إِنَّكَ مُشْرِكٌ، وَمَنَعَتْهُ الْجُلُوسَ عَلَيْهِ.

وَتَزَوَّجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ أُمُّ سَلَمَةَ وَاسْمُهَا هِنْدُ بِنْتُ أَبِي أُمِّيَّةَ بْنَ الْمُغِيرَةِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَخْزُومِ بْنِ يَقْظَةَ بْنِ مُرَّةَ بْنِ كَعْبِ بْنِ لُؤَيِّ بْنِ غَالِبٍ، وَكَانَتْ قَبْلَهُ عِنْدَ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْأَسَدِ، تُوُفِّيَتْ سَنَةَ اثْنَتَيْنِ وَسِتِّينَ، وَدُفِنَتْ بِالْبَقِيعِ، وَهِيَ آخَرُ أَزْوَاجِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ مَوْتًا، وَقِيلَ: بَلْ مَيْمُونَةُ، وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أَنَّ جِبْرِيلَ دَخَلَ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، وَهِيَ عِنْدَهُ فَرَأَتْهُ فِي صُورَةِ دِحْيَةَ الْكَلْبِيِّ. فَفِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ عَنْ أَبِي عُثْمَانَ قَالَ: أُنْبِئْتُ أَنَّ جِبْرِيلَ أَتَى النَّبِيَّ ﷺ، وَعِنْدَهُ أُمُّ سَلَمَةَ، فَقَالَ: فَجَعَلَ يَتَحَدَّثُ، ثُمَّ قَامَ فَقَالَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِأُمِّ سَلَمَةَ: "مَنْ هَذَا؟ " أَوْ كَمَا قَالَ. قَالَتْ: هَذَا دِحْيَةُ الْكَلْبِيُّ. قَالَتْ: وَايْمُ اللَّهِ، مَا حَسِبْتُهُ إِلَّا إِيَّاهُ، حَتَّى سَمِعْتُ خُطْبَةَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، يُخْبِرُ أَنَّهُ جِبْرِيلُ، أَوْ كَمَا قَالَ، قَالَ سُلَيْمَانُ التَّيْمِيُّ: فَقُلْتُ لِأَبِي عُثْمَانَ: مِمَّنْ سَمِعْتَ هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ؟ قَالَ: مِنْ أُسَامَةَ بْنِ زَيْدٍ وزوَّجها ابْنُهَا-عُمَرُ-مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَرَدَّتْ طَائِفَةٌ ذَلِكَ بِأَنَّ ابْنَهَا لَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ مِنَ السِّنِّ حِينَئِذٍ مَا يَعْقِدُ التَّزْوِيجَ، وَرَدَّ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ ذَلِكَ، وَأَنْكَرَ عَلَى مَنْ قَالَهُ، وَيَدُلُّ عَلَى صِحَّةِ قَوْلِ أَحْمَدَ مَا رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ أَنَّ عُمَرَ بْنَ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ-ابْنَهَا-سَأَلَ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ عَنِ الْقُبْلَةِ لِلصَّائِمِ؟ فَقَالَ: "سَلْ هَذِهِ" يَعْنِي: أُمَّ سَلَمَةَ فَأَخْبَرَتْهُ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَفْعَلُهُ، فَقَالَ: لَسْنَا كَرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، يُحِلُّ اللَّهُ لِرَسُولِهِ مَا شَاءَ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنِّي أَتْقَاكُمْ لِلَّهِ وَأَعْلَمُكُمْ بِهِ" أَوْ كَمَا قَالَ. وَمِثْلُ هَذَا لَا يُقَالُ لِصَغِيرٍ جِدًّا، وَعُمَرُ وُلِدَ بِأَرْضِ الْحَبَشَةِ قَبْلَ الْهِجْرَةِ. وَقَالَ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ: وَقَوْلُ مَنْ زَعَمَ أنه كان صغيرا، دَعْوَى وَلَمْ يَثْبُتْ صِغَرُهُ بِإِسْنَادٍ صَحِيحٍ.

وَتَزَوَّجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ زَيْنَبَ بِنْتَ جَحْشٍ مِنْ بَنِي خُزَيْمَةَ بْنِ مُدْرِكَةَ بْنِ إِلْيَاسَ بْنِ مُضَرَ، وَهِيَ بِنْتُ عَمَّتِهِ أُمَيْمَةَ بِنْتِ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ، وَكَانَتْ قَبْلُ عِنْدِ مَوْلَاهُ زَيْدِ بْنِ حَارِثَةَ، فَطَلَّقَهَا فَزَوَّجَهُ اللَّهُ إياها من فوق سبع سموات، وَأَنْزَلَ عَلَيْهِ: ﴿فَلَمَّا قَضَى زَيْدٌ مِنْهَا وَطَرًا زَوَّجْنَاكَهَا﴾ فَقَامَ فَدَخَلَ عَلَيْهَا بِلَا اسْتِئْذَانٍ، وَكَانَتْ تَفْخَرُ بِذَلِكَ عَلَى سَائِرُ أَزْوَاجِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، وَتَقُولُ: زوَّجكن أَهَالِيكُنَّ وزوَّجني الله من فوق سبع سمواته، وَهَذَا مِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا. تُوُفِّيَتْ بِالْمَدِينَةِ سَنَةَ عِشْرِينَ، وَدُفِنَتْ بِالْبَقِيعِ.

وَتَزَوَّجَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ زَيْنَبَ بِنْتَ خُزَيْمَةَ الْهِلَالِيَّةَ، وَكَانَتْ تَحْتَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ جَحْشٍ، تَزَوَّجَهَا سَنَةَ ثَلَاثٍ مِنَ الْهِجْرَةِ، وَكَانَتْ تُسَمَّى أَمَّ الْمَسَاكِينِ، وَلَمْ تَلْبَثْ عِنْدَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِلَّا يَسِيرًا، شَهْرَيْنِ أَوْ ثَلَاثَةً، وَتُوُفِّيَتْ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا.

وَتَزَوَّجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ جُوَيْرِيَةَ بِنْتَ الْحَارِثِ مِنْ بَنِي الْمُصْطَلِقِ، وَكَانَتْ سُبِيَتْ فِي غَزْوَةِ بَنِي الْمُصْطَلِقِ، فَوَقَعَتْ فِي سَهْمِ ثَابِتِ بْنِ قَيْسٍ، فَكَاتَبَهَا، فَقَضَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ كِتَابَتَهَا، وَتَزَوَّجَهَا سَنَةَ سِتٍّ مِنَ الْهِجْرَةِ، وَتُوُفِّيَتْ سَنَةَ سِتٍّ وَخَمْسِينَ، وَهِيَ الَّتِي أَعْتَقَ الْمُسْلِمُونَ بِسَبَبِهَا مِائَةَ أَهْلِ بَيْتٍ مِنَ الرَّقِيقِ، وَقَالُوا: أَصْهَارُ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَكَانَ ذَلِكَ مِنْ بَرَكَتِهَا عَلَى قَوْمِهَا.

وَتَزَوَّجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ صَفِيَّةَ بِنْتَ حُيَيٍّ، مِنْ وَلَدِ هَارُونَ بْنِ عِمْرَانَ أَخِي مُوسَى، سَنَةَ سَبْعٍ، فَإِنَّهَا سُبِيَتْ مِنْ خَيْبَرَ، وَكَانَتْ قَبْلَهُ تَحْتَ كِنَانَةَ بْنِ أَبِي الْحَقِيقِ، فَقَتَلَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، تُوُفِّيَتْ سَنَةَ سِتٍّ وَثَلَاثِينَ، وَقِيلَ: سَنَةَ خَمْسِينَ. وَمِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَعْتَقَهَا وَجَعَلَ عِتْقَهَا صَدَاقَهَا. قَالَ أَنَسٌ: أَمْهَرَهَا نَفْسَهَا، وَصَارَ ذَلِكَ سُنَّةً لِلْأَمَةِ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَيَجُوزُ لِلرَّجُلِ أَنْ يَجْعَلَ عِتْقَ جَارِيَتِهِ صَدَاقَهَا، وَتَصِيرُ زَوْجَتَهُ عَلَى مَنْصُوصِ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ. قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ، وَعَبْدُ بْنُ حُمَيْدٍ، قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، حَدَّثَنَا مَعْمَرٌ، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ قَالَ: بَلَغَ صَفِيَّةَ أَنَّ حَفْصَةَ قَالَتْ: صَفِيَّةُ بِنْتُ يَهُودِيٍّ، فَبَكَتْ، فَدَخَلَ عَلَيْهَا النَّبِيُّ ﷺ وَهِيَ تَبْكِي فَقَالَ: "مَا يُبْكِيكِ؟ " قَالَتْ: قَالَتْ لِي حَفْصَةُ: إِنِّي ابْنَةُ يَهُودِيٍّ. فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "إِنَّكِ لَابْنَةُ نَبِيٍّ وَإِنَّ عَمَّكِ لَنَبِيٌّ، وَإِنَّكِ لِتَحْتَ نَبِيٍّ، فَبِمَا تَفْخَرُ عَلَيْكِ؟ " ثُمَّ قَالَ: "اتَّقِ اللَّهَ يَا حَفْصَةُ". قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ صَحِيحٌ غَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ. وَهَذَا مِنْ خَصَائِصِهَا، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا.

وَتَزَوَّجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَيْمُونَةَ بِنْتَ الْحَارِثِ الْهِلَالِيَّةَ، تَزَوَّجَهَا بسَرَف وَهُوَ عَلَى تِسْعَةِ أَمْيَالٍ مِنْ مَكَّةَ، وَهِيَ آخِرُ مَنْ تَزَوَّجَ مِنْ أُمَّهَاتِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، تُوُفِّيَتْ سَنَةَ ثَلَاثٍ وَسِتِّينَ، وَهِيَ خَالَةُ خَالِدِ بْنِ الْوَلِيدِ، وَخَالَةُ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، فَإِنَّ أُمَّهُ أُمُّ الْفَضْلِ بِنْتُ الْحَارِثِ وَهِيَ الَّتِي اخْتُلِفَ فِي نِكَاحِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ لَهَا. هَلْ نَكَحَهَا حَلَالًا أَوْ مُحرمًا؟ وَالصَّحِيحُ إِنَّمَا تَزَوَّجَهَا حَلَالًا كَمَا قَالَ أَبُو رَافِعٍ الشَّفِيرُ فِي نِكَاحِهَا.

قَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو مُحَمَّدٍ الْمَقْدِسِيُّ وَغَيْرُهُ: وَعَقَدَ عَلَى سَبْعٍ وَلَمْ يَدْخُلْ بِهِنَّ، فَالصَّلَاةُ عَلَى أَزْوَاجِهِ تَابِعَةٌ لِاحْتِرَامِهِنَّ وَتَحْرِيمِهِنَّ عَلَى الْأُمَّةِ، وَأَنَّهُنَّ نِسَاؤُهُ ﷺ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، فَمَنْ فَارَقَهَا فِي حَيَاتِهَا وَلَمْ يَدْخُلْ، لَا يَثْبُتُ لَهَا أَحْكَامُ زَوْجَاتِهِ اللَّاتِي دَخَلَ بِهِنَّ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وعلى أزواجه وآله وذريته وسلم تسليما] .

---

## 33:30-31 — verses 30-31 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, admonishing the wives of the Prophet ﷺ, those who chose God, His Messenger, and the Final Abode, and whose affair became settled under the Messenger of God ﷺ, that He would inform them of their ruling and their being singled out beyond all other women: that whoever among them commits a manifest indecency... Ibn Abbas said: this refers to nushuz (marital defiance) and bad character. In any case, this is a conditional statement, and a condition does not necessitate its actual occurrence, like His saying: {And it has already been revealed to you and to those before you: if you associate partners with God, your deeds will surely become worthless} [al-Zumar: 65], and like His saying: {But if they had associated partners with God, all that they used to do would have been worthless for them} [al-An'am: 88], {Say: if the Most Merciful had a son, then I would be the first of worshippers} [al-Zukhruf: 81], {If God had wanted to take a son, He would have chosen from what He creates whatever He willed. Glory be to Him. He is God, the One, the Overpowering} [al-Zumar: 4]. Since their station was elevated, it was fitting that, were a sin to occur from them, it be made grave, as a safeguarding of their sanctity and their elevated veil. For this reason He said: {Whoever among you commits a manifest indecency, the punishment will be doubled for her twofold}.

Malik said, on the authority of Zayd ibn Aslam, regarding {the punishment will be doubled for her twofold}: he said, in this world and the Hereafter.

And from Ibn Abi Najih [from Mujahid], the same.

{And that is easy for God} means: simple and effortless for Him.

Then He mentions His justice and His favor in His saying: {And whoever among you is devoutly obedient to God and His Messenger} meaning: obeys God and His Messenger and responds, {We will give her reward twice, and We have prepared for her a generous provision} meaning: in Paradise. For they will be in the dwellings of the Messenger of God ﷺ, in the highest of Illiyyun (the highest ranks), above the dwellings of all created beings, in al-Wasilah (the intermediary station), which is the closest of the dwellings of Paradise to the Throne.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى وَاعِظًا نِسَاءَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، اللَّاتِي اخْتَرْنَ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالدَّارَ الْآخِرَةَ، وَاسْتَقَرَّ أَمْرُهُنَّ تَحْتَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنْ يُخْبِرَهُنَّ بِحُكْمِهِنَّ [وَتَخْصِيصِهِنَّ] دُونَ سَائِرِ النِّسَاءِ، بِأَنَّ مَنْ يَأْتِ مِنْهُنَّ بِفَاحِشَةٍ مُبَيِّنَةٍ -قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: وَهِيَ النُّشُوزُ وَسُوءُ الْخُلُقِ. وَعَلَى كُلِّ تَقْدِيرٍ فَهُوَ شَرْطٌ، وَالشَّرْطُ لَا يَقْتَضِي الْوُقُوعَ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ أُوحِيَ إِلَيْكَ وَإِلَى الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ لَئِنْ أَشْرَكْتَ لَيَحْبَطَنَّ عَمَلُكَ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ:٦٥] ، وَكَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَوْ أَشْرَكُوا لَحَبِطَ عَنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٨٨] ، ﴿قُلْ إِنْ كَانَ لِلرَّحْمَنِ وَلَدٌ فَأَنَا أَوَّلُ الْعَابِدِينَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ:٨١] ، ﴿لَوْ أَرَادَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَتَّخِذَ وَلَدًا لاصْطَفَى مِمَّا يَخْلُقُ مَا يَشَاءُ سُبْحَانَهُ هُوَ اللَّهُ الْوَاحِدُ الْقَهَّارُ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ:٤] ، فَلَمَّا كَانَتْ محلَّتهن رَفِيعَةً، نَاسَبَ أَنْ يَجْعَلَ الذَّنْبَ لَوْ وَقَعَ مِنْهُنَّ مُغْلَّظًا، صِيَانَةً لِجَنَابِهِنَّ وَحِجَابِهِنَّ الرَّفِيعِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿مَنْ يَأْتِ مِنْكُنَّ بِفَاحِشَةٍ مُبَيِّنَةٍ يُضَاعَفْ لَهَا الْعَذَابُ ضِعْفَيْنِ﴾ .

قَالَ مَالِكٌ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: ﴿يُضَاعَفْ لَهَا الْعَذَابُ ضِعْفَيْنِ﴾ قَالَ: فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ.

وَعَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي نَجِيحٍ [عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ] مِثْلَهُ.

﴿وَكَانَ ذَلِكَ عَلَى اللَّهِ يَسِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: سَهْلًا هَيِّنًا.

ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ عَدْلَهُ وَفَضْلَهُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَنْ يَقْنُتْ مِنْكُنَّ لِلَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ﴾ أَيْ: يُطِعِ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَيَسْتَجِبْ ﴿نُؤْتِهَا أَجْرَهَا مَرَّتَيْنِ وَأَعْتَدْنَا لَهَا رِزْقًا كَرِيمًا﴾ أَيْ: فِي الْجَنَّةِ، فَإِنَّهُنَّ فِي مَنَازِلِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فِي أَعْلَى عِلِّيِّينَ، فَوْقَ مَنَازِلِ جَمِيعِ الْخَلَائِقِ، فِي الْوَسِيلَةِ الَّتِي هي أقرب منازل الجنة إلى العرش.

---

## 33:32-34 — verses 32-34 (shared commentary)

### Translation

These are proprieties which God, exalted is He, commanded the wives of the Prophet ﷺ, and the women of the ummah follow them in this. He said, addressing the wives of the Prophet [ﷺ], that if they feared God as He commanded them, then no woman would resemble them, nor would anyone attain their level in virtue and standing. Then He said: {So do not be soft in speech}.

Al-Suddi and others said: this means softening the speech when they address men. Hence He said: {lest he in whose heart is disease should be moved with desire}, that is, corruption, {but speak a words of correctness}. Ibn Zayd said: good, pleasant speech, recognized as proper in what is good.

The meaning of this is that a woman should address unrelated men with speech that has no softness or coquetry in it, that is, a woman should not address unrelated men as she addresses her husband.

And His saying: {And stay in your houses} means: remain in your houses and do not go out except for need. Among the legitimate needs is prayer in the mosque under its conditions, as the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Do not prevent the female servants of God from the mosques of God, and let them go out unperfumed." And in another version: "and their houses are better for them."

The hadith master Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: [chain] Humayd ibn Mas'ada told us, Abu Raja' al-Kalbi told us, Rawh ibn al-Musayyab being trustworthy, Thabit al-Bunani told us from Anas, may God be pleased with him, who said: the women came to the Messenger of God ﷺ and said: O Messenger of God, the men have gone off with the merit and with jihad in the way of God, exalted is He, so what deed do we have by which we can attain the deed of those who strive in the way of God? The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Whoever among you sits" or a similar phrase "in her house, she attains the deed of those who strive in the way of God."

Then he said: we do not know of anyone who narrated it from Thabit except Rawh ibn al-Musayyab, who is a well known man from the people of Basra.

Al-Bazzar also said: [chain] Muhammad ibn al-Muthanna told us, 'Amr ibn 'Asim told us, Hammam told us, from Qatada, from Muwarriq, from Abu al-Ahwas, from 'Abd Allah, from the Prophet ﷺ who said: "The woman is a private matter (private thing to be concealed), and when she goes out, Satan looks upon her with keen interest, and she is nearest to the mercy of her Lord when she is in the depth of her house."

Al-Tirmidhi narrated it from Bundar, from 'Amr ibn 'Asim, with something similar.

Al-Bazzar narrated by the chain given above, and Abu Dawud also narrated, from the Prophet ﷺ who said: "The prayer of a woman in her inner chamber is better than her prayer in her house, and her prayer in her house is better than her prayer in her courtyard." This is a good chain.

Regarding His saying, exalted is He: {and do not display yourselves as the display of the former Age of Ignorance}, Mujahid said: a woman would go out walking ahead of the men, and that was the display of the Age of Ignorance.

Qatada said: {and do not display yourselves as the display of the former Age of Ignorance} means: when you go out of your houses, and they had a certain gait, an affected swaying and coquettish manner, God forbade that.

Muqatil ibn Hayyan said: {and do not display yourselves as the display of the former Age of Ignorance}: display (tabarruj) means that a woman would throw her head-covering over her head without fastening it, so that it would not cover her necklaces, earrings, and neck, and all of that would show from her. That is display. Then this description came to apply generally to the believing women regarding display. Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ibn Zuhayr told me, Musa ibn Isma'il told us, Dawud, that is ibn Abi al-Furat, told us, 'Ali ibn Ahmar told us, from 'Ikrima, from Ibn 'Abbas who said: he recited this verse, {and do not display yourselves as the display of the former Age of Ignorance}, and said: that was in the period between Noah and Idris (peace be upon them), a period of a thousand years. There were two tribes among the descendants of Adam, one of which lived in the plain and the other in the mountain. The men of the mountain were handsome while their women were plain, and the women of the plain were beautiful while their men were plain. Iblis came to a man of the people of the plain in the form of a young servant, and hired himself out to him, so he served him. Iblis fashioned something like the pipe that shepherds play, and produced from it a sound the like of which people had never heard. That reached those around him, so they came repeatedly to listen to it, and they made it into a festival to which they gathered once a year, and the women would display themselves to the men there. He said: and the men would adorn themselves for the women. Then a man from the people of the mountain came upon them suddenly during that festival of theirs, and he saw the women and their beauty, so he went to his companions and told them of this, and they moved to be near them and settled among them, and lewdness appeared among them. That is the meaning of His saying, exalted is He: {and do not display yourselves as the display of the former Age of Ignorance}.

Regarding His saying: {and establish prayer and give zakat and obey God and His Messenger}, He first forbade them from evil, then commanded them to good, from the establishment of prayer, which is the worship of God alone without partner, and the giving of zakat, which is kindness to created beings, {and obey God and His Messenger}, and this is an instance of joining the general to the specific. And His saying: {God only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the House, and to purify you with a thorough purification}: this is an explicit text for the inclusion of the wives of the Prophet ﷺ among the People of the House here, because they were the occasion for the revelation of this verse, and the occasion of revelation is included in the verse without any dispute, whether it applies to it alone according to one opinion, or together with others according to the correct view.

Ibn Jarir narrated from 'Ikrima that he used to call out in the marketplace: {God only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the House, and to purify you with a thorough purification} was revealed regarding the wives of the Prophet ﷺ specifically. Ibn Abi Hatim likewise narrated, saying:

[chain] 'Ali ibn Harb al-Mawsili told us, Zayd ibn al-Hubab told us, Husayn ibn Waqid told us, from Yazid al-Nahwi, from 'Ikrima, from Ibn 'Abbas, regarding His saying: {God only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the House}, he said: it was revealed regarding the wives of the Prophet ﷺ specifically.

'Ikrima said: whoever wishes, I will make a solemn pledge with him that it was revealed regarding the wives of the Prophet ﷺ.

If what is meant is that they were the occasion of the revelation apart from others, that is correct. But if what is meant is that they alone are intended, to the exclusion of others, there is room for question in this, for there have come hadiths indicating that what is meant is broader than that:

The first hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] 'Affan told us, Hammad told us, 'Ali ibn Zayd informed us, from Anas ibn Malik, may God be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ used to pass by the door of Fatima for six months, when he went out to the dawn prayer, saying: "Prayer, O people of the House! {God only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the House, and to purify you with a thorough purification}."

Al-Tirmidhi narrated it from 'Abd ibn Humayd, from 'Affan, with the same content, and said: hasan gharib (sound but singular in transmission).

Another hadith: Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ibn Wakia told us, Abu Nu'aym told us, Yunus ibn Abi Ishaq told us, Abu Dawud informed me, from Abu al-Hamra' who said: I kept watch at Medina for seven months in the time of the Messenger of God ﷺ. [He said: I saw the Messenger of God ﷺ], when dawn broke, come to the door of 'Ali and Fatima and say: "Prayer, prayer! {God only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the House, and to purify you with a thorough purification}."

Abu Dawud al-A'ma is Nufay' ibn al-Harith, a liar (kadhdhab).

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Mus'ab told us, al-Awza'i told us, Shaddad Abu 'Ammar told us, who said: I went in to Wathila ibn al-Asqa', and there were people with him, and they mentioned 'Ali, may God be pleased with him. When they got up, he said to me: shall I not tell you of what I saw from the Messenger of God ﷺ? I said: yes indeed. He said: I went to Fatima to ask her about 'Ali, and she said: he has gone to the Messenger of God ﷺ. So I sat waiting for him until the Messenger of God ﷺ came, with him 'Ali, Hasan, and Husayn, holding each of them by the hand, until he entered. He drew 'Ali and Fatima close and seated them before him, and he seated Hasan and Husayn each on one of his thighs, then he wrapped his garment, or he said his cloak, over them, then he recited this verse: {God only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the House, and to purify you with a thorough purification}, saying: "O God, these are the people of my House, and the people of my House have greater right." Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir also narrated it from 'Abd al-Karim ibn Abi 'Umayr, from al-Walid ibn Muslim, from Abu 'Amr al-Awza'i, with his chain, similarly, adding at the end: Wathila said: I said: and am I, O Messenger of God, may God's blessings be upon you, among your family? He said: "You too are of my family." Wathila said: it is among the things I most hope for.

Then he also related it, from Abd al-A'la ibn Wasil, from al-Fadl ibn Dukayn, from Abd al-Salam ibn Harb, from Kulthum al-Muharibi, from Shaddad Abu Ammar, who said: I was sitting with Wathila ibn al-Asqa' when they mentioned Ali and reviled him. When they got up, he said: Sit, so that I may tell you about the one they reviled. I was with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ when Ali, Fatima, Hasan and Husayn came, and he ﷺ threw over them a cloak of his, then said: "O Allah, these are the people of my house. O Allah, remove impurity from them and purify them completely." I said: O Messenger of Allah, and me? He said: "And you." He said: By Allah, that is the most secure of my deeds in my own eyes.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Abdullah ibn Numayr told us, Abd al-Malik ibn Abi Sulayman told us, from Ata ibn Abi Rabah, who said: someone who heard Umm Salama told me that she related that the Prophet ﷺ was in her house, and Fatima, may Allah be pleased with her, brought him a pot containing khazira (a kind of porridge), and entered with it to him. He said to her: "Call your husband and your two sons." She said: So Ali, Hasan and Husayn came and entered upon him, and they sat eating from that khazira, while he was on a sleeping mat of his on a raised platform, under him a Khaybari cloak. She said: I was in the chamber praying, and Allah, Mighty and Majestic, sent down this verse: {Allah only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the house, and to purify you completely}. She said: He took the extra part of the cloak and covered them with it, then put out his hand and gestured with it toward the sky, then said: "O Allah, these are the people of my house and my close ones, so remove impurity from them and purify them completely." She said: I put my head into the house and said: And am I with you, O Messenger of Allah? He said: "You are heading toward good, you are heading toward good."

In its chain of transmission there is someone unnamed, who is the teacher of Ata, but the rest of its men are trustworthy.

Another route: Imam Ahmad said: Muhammad ibn Ja'far told us, Awf told us, from Abu al-Mu'addil, from Atiyya al-Tufawi, from his father, that Umm Salama told him, saying: While the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was in my house one day, the servant said: Fatima and Ali are at the doorway. She said: He said to me: "Get up and move away from the people of my house." She said: So I got up and moved aside within the house, nearby, and Ali and Fatima entered, with them Hasan and Husayn, who were two small boys. He took the two boys and placed them in his lap and kissed them, and he embraced Ali with one of his hands and Fatima with the other hand, and he kissed Fatima and kissed Ali, and he draped over them a black khamisa (woolen garment) and said: "O Allah, to You, not to the Fire, myself and the people of my house." She said: I said: And me, O Messenger of Allah? May Allah's blessings be upon you. He said: "And you."

Another route: Ibn Jarir said: Abu Kurayb told us, [al-Hasan ibn Atiyya told us, from] Fudayl ibn Marzuq, from Atiyya, from Abu Sa'id, from Umm Salama, that this verse was sent down in her house: {Allah only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the house, and to purify you completely}. She said: I was sitting at the door of the house, and I said: O Messenger of Allah, am I not among the people of the house? He said: "You are heading toward good, you are among the wives of the Prophet ﷺ." She said: And in the house were the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, Ali, Fatima, Hasan and Husayn, may Allah be pleased with them.

Another route: Ibn Jarir also related it, from Abu Kurayb, from Waki', from Abd al-Hamid ibn Bahram, from Shahr ibn Hawshab, from Umm Salama, similarly.

Another route: Ibn Jarir said: Abu Kurayb told us, Khalid ibn Makhlad told us, Musa ibn Ya'qub told me, Hashim ibn Hashim ibn Utba ibn Abi Waqqas told me, from Abdullah ibn Wahb ibn Zam'a, who said: Umm Salama, may Allah be pleased with her, informed me that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ gathered Fatima, Hasan and Husayn, then brought them under his garment, then cried out to Allah, Mighty and Majestic, then said: "These are the people of my house." Umm Salama said: I said: O Messenger of Allah, bring me in with them. He said: "You are among my household."

Another route: Ibn Jarir also related it, from Ahmad ibn Muhammad al-Tusi, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Salih, from Muhammad ibn Sulayman al-Asbahani, from Yahya ibn Ubayd al-Makki, from Ata, from Umar ibn Abi Salama, from his mother, similarly to that.

Another route: Ibn Jarir said: Abu Kurayb told us, Mus'ab ibn al-Miqdam told us, Sa'id ibn Zarbi told us, from Muhammad ibn Sirin, from Abu Hurayra, from Umm Salama, who said: Fatima came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ with a pot of hers in which she had made asida (a kind of dish), carrying it on a tray, and she set it before him. He said: "Where is your cousin and your two sons?" She said: In the house. He said: "Call them." So she went to Ali and said: Answer the Messenger of Allah, you and your two sons. Umm Salama said: When he saw them approaching, he stretched out his hand to a cloak that was on the sleeping mat, spread it out, and seated them on it. Then he took the four corners of the cloak with his left hand and gathered it over their heads, and gestured with his right hand toward his Lord, Mighty and Majestic, and said: "O Allah, these are the people of my house, so remove impurity from them and purify them completely."

Another route: Ibn Jarir said: Ibn Humayd told us, Abdullah ibn Abd al-Qudus told us, from al-A'mash, from Hakim ibn Sa'd, who said: We mentioned Ali ibn Abi Talib in the presence of Umm Salama, and she said: It was in my house that this was sent down: {Allah only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the house, and to purify you completely}. Umm Salama said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ came to my house and said: "Do not admit anyone." Then Fatima came, and I was not able to keep her away from her father. Then Hasan came, and I was not able to keep him away from his mother and grandfather. Then Husayn came, and I was not able to keep him away. Then Ali came, and I was not able to keep him away. So they gathered together, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ covered them with a cloak that was upon him, then said: "These are the people of my house, so remove impurity from them and purify them completely." Then this verse came down when they had gathered upon the spread. She said: I said: O Messenger of Allah, and me? She said: By Allah, he did not grant that, and he said: "You are heading toward good."

Another hadith: Ibn Jarir said: Ibn Waki' told us, Muhammad ibn Bishr told us, from Zakariyya, from Mus'ab ibn Shayba, from Safiyya bint Shayba, who said: Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ went out one morning wearing a striped mirt (cloak) of black hair. Hasan came, and he brought him in with him. Then Husayn came, and he brought him in with him. Then Fatima came, and he brought her in with him. Then Ali came, and he brought him in with him. Then he said: {Allah only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the house, and to purify you completely}.

Muslim related it from Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shayba, from Muhammad ibn Bishr, with it.

Another route: Ibn Abi Hatim said: My father told us, Surayj ibn Yunus Abu al-Harith told us, Muhammad ibn Yazid told us, from al-Awwam, meaning ibn Hawshab, from an uncle of his, who said: I entered with my father upon Aisha, and I asked her about Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, and she, may Allah be pleased with her, said: You ask me about a man who was among the most beloved of people to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and whose wife was his daughter, the most beloved of people to him? I indeed saw the Messenger of Allah ﷺ call Ali, Fatima, Hasan and Husayn, and throw over them a garment, and say: "O Allah, these are the people of my house, so remove impurity from them and purify them completely." She said: I drew near to him and said: O Messenger of Allah, and am I among the people of your house? He said: "Move aside, for you are upon good."

Another hadith: Ibn Jarir said: al-Muthanna told us, Bakr ibn Yahya ibn Zabban al-Anazi told us, Mandal told us, from al-A'mash, from Atiyya, from Abu Sa'id, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "This verse came down concerning five: concerning me, and concerning Ali, Hasan, Husayn, and Fatima: {Allah only wishes to remove impurity from you, O people of the house, and to purify you completely}."

It has already been mentioned that Fudayl ibn Marzuq related it from Atiyya, from Abu Sa'id, from Umm Salama, as previously noted.

And Ibn Abi Hatim related, from the hadith of Harun ibn Sa'd al-Ijli, from Atiyya, from Abu Sa'id, as a mawquf (halted report). And Allah knows best.

Another hadith: Ibn Jarir said: Ibn al-Muthanna narrated to us, Abu Bakr al-Hanafi narrated to us, Bukayr ibn Mismar narrated to us, he said: I heard Amir ibn Sa'd say: Sa'd said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, when the revelation descended upon him, taking Ali and his two sons and Fatima and bringing them under his garment, then he said: "O Lord, these are my family and the people of my house."

Another hadith: Muslim said in his Sahih: Zuhayr ibn Harb and Shuja' ibn Makhlad both narrated to me, from Ibn Ulayyah, Zuhayr said: Isma'il ibn Ibrahim narrated to us, Abu Hayyan narrated to me, Yazid ibn Hayyan narrated to me, he said: I set out, along with Husayn ibn Sabrah and Umar ibn Muslim, to Zayd ibn Arqam. When we sat with him, Husayn said to him: You have indeed encountered much good, O Zayd. [You saw the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and heard his speech, and fought alongside him, and prayed behind him. You have indeed encountered much good, O Zayd.] Tell us, O Zayd, what you heard from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. He said: O son of my brother, by Allah, my age has grown great, my time has grown distant, and I have forgotten some of what I used to retain from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. So whatever I narrate to you, accept it, and whatever I do not, do not burden me with it. Then he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ stood among us one day delivering a sermon at a water source called Khumm, between Mecca and Medina. He praised Allah and extolled Him, exhorted and reminded, then said: "To proceed: O people, I am only a human being. The messenger of my Lord is about to come to me and I will respond. I am leaving among you two weighty things. The first of them is the Book of Allah, in which is guidance and light. So take hold of the Book of Allah and hold fast to it." He urged them toward the Book of Allah and encouraged it, then said: "And the people of my house. I remind you of Allah regarding the people of my house. I remind you of Allah regarding the people of my house." Three times. Husayn said to him: Who are the people of his house, O Zayd? Are not his wives among the people of his house? He said: His wives are among the people of his house, but the people of his house are those who are forbidden from receiving charity after him. He said: And who are they? He said: They are the family of Ali, the family of Aqil, the family of Ja'far, and the family of Abbas. He said: Are all of these forbidden from receiving charity? He said: Yes.

Then he narrated it from Muhammad ibn Bakkar ibn al-Rayyan, from Hassan ibn Ibrahim, from Sa'id ibn Masruq, from Yazid ibn Hayyan, from Zayd ibn Arqam, and he mentioned the hadith similarly to what preceded, and in it: We said to him: Who are the people of his house? Are they his wives? He said: No, by Allah. A woman remains with a man for a period of time, then he divorces her, and she returns to her father and her people. The people of his house are his lineage and his kinsmen (asabah), those who were forbidden from receiving charity after him.

This is how it occurs in this narration, but the first is preferable, and adopting it is more fitting. This second narration could be understood as meaning that he intended to explain the "family" mentioned in the hadith he narrated, namely that what is meant by them is his kinsmen who were forbidden from charity, or that what is meant by "family" is not the wives alone, but rather they along with his kinsmen. This latter possibility is more likely, reconciling this narration with the one before it, and also reconciling the Qur'an with the preceding hadiths if they are authentic, for there is something questionable in some of their chains of transmission. And Allah knows best. Then, what no one who reflects on the Qur'an doubts is that the wives of the Prophet ﷺ are included in His statement, the Exalted: {Allah only wishes to remove impurity from you, People of the House, and to purify you with a thorough purification}, for the context of the speech is addressed to them. This is why Allah, the Exalted, said after all this: {And remember what is recited in your houses of the verses of Allah and wisdom}, meaning: act upon what Allah sends down to His Messenger in your houses, from the Book and the Sunnah. This was said by Qatadah and more than one other. And remember this blessing with which you were singled out among the people, that revelation descends in your houses and not in the houses of other people. Aisha [al-Siddiqah, the truthful woman], daughter of al-Siddiq, is the most deserving of them of this blessing, the most fortunate of them in this bounty, and the most specially favored of them with this all-encompassing mercy, for revelation never descended upon the Messenger of Allah ﷺ in the bed of any woman other than her, as he himself stated explicitly ﷺ. Some of the scholars, may Allah have mercy on him, said: because he never married a virgin other than her, and no man ever slept with her in her bed other than him, so it was fitting that she be singled out with this distinction, and that she alone be given this exalted rank. But if his wives are among the people of his house, then his kinsmen have a greater right to this designation, as stated previously in the hadith: "And the people of my house have a greater right." This resembles what is established in Sahih Muslim: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, when asked about the mosque that was founded upon piety from the first day, said: "It is this mosque of mine." This is of the same kind, for the verse was actually revealed concerning the mosque of Quba, as reported in other hadiths. But if that mosque was founded upon piety from the first day, then the mosque of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ has a greater right to be so named. And Allah knows best.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Jamilah said: When Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, was killed, al-Hasan ibn Ali was appointed as successor. He said: While he was praying, a man leaped upon him and stabbed him with a dagger.
