يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ نَبِيِّهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، إِنَّهُ قَالَ لِمَوْلَاهُ زَيْدِ بْنِ حَارِثَةَ وَهُوَ الَّذِي أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ، أَيْ: بِالْإِسْلَامِ، وَمُتَابَعَةِ الرَّسُولِ، عَلَيْهِ أَفْضَلُ الصَّلَاةِ وَالسَّلَامِ: ﴿وَأَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْه﴾ أَيْ: بِالْعِتْقِ مِنَ الرِّقِّ، وَكَانَ سَيِّدًا كَبِيرَ الشَّأْنِ جَلِيلَ الْقَدْرِ، حَبِيبًا إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، يُقَالُ لَهُ: الحِبّ، وَيُقَالُ لِابْنِهِ أُسَامَةَ: الحِبّ ابْنُ الحِبّ. قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا: مَا بَعَثَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي سَرِيَّةٍ إِلَّا أَمَّرَهُ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَلَوْ عَاشَ بَعْدَهُ لَاسْتَخْلَفَهُ. رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ الْوَرَّاقِ وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُبَيْدٍ، عَنْ وَائِلِ بْنِ دَاوُدَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْبَهِيِّ عَنْهَا .

وَقَالَ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا خَالِدُ بْنُ يُوسُفَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَوَانة (ح) ، وَحَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مَعْمَر، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو دَاوُدَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَوَانَةَ، أَخْبَرَنِي عِمْرَانُ بْنُ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ: حَدَّثَنِي أُسَامَةُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ قَالَ: كُنْتُ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، فَأَتَانِي الْعَبَّاسُ وَعَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، فَقَالَا يَا أُسَامَةَ، اسْتَأْذِنْ لَنَا على رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم. قَالَ: فأتيتُ رسولَ اللَّهِ فَأَخْبَرْتُهُ، فَقُلْتُ: عَلِيٌّ وَالْعَبَّاسُ يَسْتَأْذِنَانِ؟ فَقَالَ: "أَتَدْرِي مَا حَاجَتُهُمَا؟ " قُلْتُ: لَا يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ. فَقَالَ: "لَكِنِّي أَدْرِي"، قَالَ: فَأَذِنَ لَهُمَا. قَالَا يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، جِئْنَاكَ لِتُخْبِرَنَا: أيُّ أَهْلِكَ أحبُّ إِلَيْكَ؟ فَقَالَ: "أَحَبُّ أَهْلِي إليَّ فَاطِمَةُ بِنْتُ مُحَمَّدٍ" قَالَا يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا نَسْأَلُكَ عَنْ فَاطِمَةَ. قَالَ: "فَأُسَامَةُ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ حَارِثَةَ، الَّذِي أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وَأَنْعَمْتُ عَلَيْهِ" .

وَكَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَدْ زَوّجه بِابْنَةِ عَمَّتِهِ زَيْنَبَ بِنْتِ جَحْشٍ الْأَسَدِيَّةِ -وَأُمُّهَا أُمَيْمَةُ بِنْتُ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ -وَأَصْدَقَهَا عَشَرَةَ دَنَانِيرَ، وَسِتِّينَ دِرْهَمًا، وخِمارا، ومِلْحَفة، ودرْعًا، وَخَمْسِينَ مُدّا مِنْ طَعَامٍ، وَعَشْرَةَ أَمْدَادٍ مِنْ تَمْرٍ. قَالَهُ مُقَاتِلُ بْنُ حَيَّانَ، فَمَكَثْتُ عِنْدَهُ قَرِيبًا مِنْ سَنَةٍ أَوْ فَوْقَهَا، ثُمَّ وَقَعَ بَيْنَهُمَا، فَجَاءَ زَيْدٌ يَشْكُوهَا إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَجَعَلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ يَقُولُ لَهُ: "أَمْسِكْ عَلَيْكَ زَوْجَكَ، وَاتَّقِ اللَّهَ". قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتُخْفِي فِي نَفْسِكَ مَا اللَّهُ مُبْدِيهِ وَتَخْشَى النَّاسَ وَاللَّهُ أَحَقُّ أَنْ تَخْشَاهُ﴾ .

ذَكَرَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ هَاهُنَا آثَارًا عَنْ بَعْضِ السَّلَفِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ، أَحْبَبْنَا أن نضرب عَنْهَا صفَحا لِعَدَمِ صِحَّتِهَا فَلَا نُورِدُهَا.

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ هَاهُنَا أَيْضًا حَدِيثًا، مِنْ رِوَايَةِ حَمَّادُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ فِيهِ غَرَابَةٌ تَرَكْنَا سِيَاقَهُ أَيْضًا .

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْبُخَارِيُّ أَيْضًا بَعْضَهُ مُخْتَصَرًا فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحِيمِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعَلَّى بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا ثَابِتٌ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ قَالَ: إِنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿وَتُخْفِي فِي نَفْسِكَ مَا اللَّهُ مُبْدِيهِ﴾ نَزَلَتْ فِي شَأْنِ زَيْنَبَ بِنْتِ جَحْشٍ، وَزَيْدِ بْنِ حَارِثَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ هَاشِمِ بْنِ مَرْزُوقٍ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ جُدْعان قَالَ: سَأَلَنِي عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ مَا يَقُولُ الْحَسَنُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَتُخْفِي فِي نَفْسِكَ مَا اللَّهُ مُبْدِيهِ [وَتَخْشَى النَّاسَ وَاللَّهُ أَحَقُّ أَنْ تَخْشَاهُ] ﴾ ؟ فَذَكَرْتُ لَهُ فَقَالَ: لَا وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ أَعْلَمَ نَبِيَّهُ أَنَّهَا سَتَكُونُ مِنْ أَزْوَاجِهِ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَتَزَوَّجَهَا، فَلَمَّا أَتَاهُ زَيْدٌ لِيَشْكُوَهَا إِلَيْهِ قَالَ: اتَّقِ اللَّهَ، وَأَمْسِكْ عَلَيْكَ زَوْجَكَ. فَقَالَ: قَدْ أَخْبَرْتُكَ أَنِّي مُزَوّجكها، وَتُخْفِي فِي نَفْسِكَ مَا اللَّهُ مُبْدِيهِ.

وَهَكَذَا رُوي عَنِ السُّدِّي أَنَّهُ قَالَ نَحْوَ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ شَاهِينَ، حَدَّثَنِي خَالِدٌ، عَنْ دَاوُدَ عَنْ عَامِرٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ: لَوْ كَتَمَ مُحَمَّدٌ ﷺ شَيْئًا مِمَّا أُوحِيَ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ، لِكَتَمَ: ﴿وَتُخْفِي فِي نَفْسِكَ مَا اللَّهُ مُبْدِيهِ وَتَخْشَى النَّاسَ وَاللَّهُ أَحَقُّ أَنْ تَخْشَاهُ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَلَمَّا قَضَى زَيْدٌ مِنْهَا وَطَرًا زَوَّجْنَاكَهَا﴾ : الْوَطَرُ: هُوَ الْحَاجَةُ وَالْأَرَبُ، أَيْ: لَمَّا فَرَغ مِنْهَا، وَفَارَقَهَا، زَوّجناكها، وَكَانَ الَّذِي وَلي تَزْوِيجَهَا مِنْهُ هُوَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، بِمَعْنَى: أَنَّهُ أَوْحَى إِلَيْهِ أَنْ يَدْخُلَ عَلَيْهَا بِلَا وَلِيٍّ وَلَا مَهْرٍ وَلَا عَقْدٍ وَلَا شُهُودٍ مِنَ الْبَشَرِ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا هَاشِمٌ -يَعْنِي: ابْنُ الْقَاسِمِ أَبُو النَّضْرِ -حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ الْمُغِيرَةَ، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: لَمَّا انْقَضَتْ عِدَّةُ زَيْنَبَ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِزَيْدِ بْنِ حَارِثَةَ: "اذْهَبْ فَاذْكُرْهَا عَلَيَّ". فَانْطَلَقَ حَتَّى أَتَاهَا وَهِيَ تُخَمِّر عَجينها، قَالَ: فَلَمَّا رَأَيْتُهَا عَظُمَتْ فِي صَدْرِي -حَتَّى مَا أَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ أَنْظُرَ إِلَيْهَا -أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ ذَكَرَهَا، فَوَلَّيْتُهَا ظَهْرِي وَنَكَصْتُ عَلَى عَقِبِي، وَقُلْتُ: يَا زَيْنَبُ، أَبْشِرِي، أَرْسَلَنِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَذْكُرُكِ. قَالَتْ: ما أنا بصانعة شيئا حتى أُؤَامِرَ رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ. فَقَامَتْ إِلَى مَسْجِدِهَا، وَنَزَلَ الْقُرْآنُ، وَجَاءَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَدَخَلَ عَلَيْهَا بِغَيْرِ إِذْنٍ. وَلَقَدْ رَأَيْتُنَا حِينَ دَخَلَتْ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَطْعَمَنَا عَلَيْهَا الْخُبْزَ وَاللَّحْمَ، فَخَرَجَ النَّاسُ وَبَقِيَ رِجَالٌ يَتَحَدَّثُونَ فِي الْبَيْتِ بَعْدَ الطَّعَامِ، فَخَرَجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ [وَاتَّبَعَتْهُ] فَجَعَلَ يَتَتَبَّعُ حُجر نِسَائِهِ يُسَلِّمُ عَلَيْهِنَّ، وَيَقُلْنَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، كَيْفَ وَجَدْتَ أَهْلَكَ؟ فَمَا أَدْرِي أَنَا أَخْبَرْتُهُ أَنَّ الْقَوْمَ قَدْ خَرَجُوا أَوْ أُخْبِرَ. قَالَ: فَانْطَلَقَ حَتَّى دَخَلَ الْبَيْتَ، فَذَهَبْتُ أَدْخَلَ مَعَهُ، فَأَلْقَى السِّتْرَ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَهُ، وَنَزَلَ الْحِجَابُ، وَوَعَظَ الْقَوْمَ بِمَا وُعِظُوا بِهِ: ﴿لَا تَدْخُلُوا بُيُوتَ النَّبِيِّ إِلا أَنْ يُؤْذَنَ لَكُمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ الْمُغِيرَةِ، بِهِ. 

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْبُخَارِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ زَيْنَبَ بِنْتَ جَحْشٍ كَانَتْ تَفْخَرُ عَلَى أَزْوَاجِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَتَقُولُ: زَوَّجَكُنَّ أهاليكن وزوجني الله من فوق سبع سموات .

وَقَدْ قَدَّمْنَا فِي "سُورَةِ النُّورِ" عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ جَحْشٍ قَالَ: تَفَاخَرَتْ زَيْنَبُ وَعَائِشَةُ، فَقَالَتْ زَيْنَبُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا : أَنَا الَّتِي نَزَلَ تَزْوِيجِي مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، وَقَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: أَنَا الَّتِي نَزَلَ عُذْري مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، فَاعْتَرَفَتْ لَهَا زَيْنَبُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا. 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرٌ، عَنِ الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ قَالَ: كَانَتْ زَيْنَبُ تَقُولُ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ إِنِّي لَأَدِلُّ عَلَيْكَ بِثَلَاثٍ، مَا مِنْ نِسَائِكَ امْرَأَةٌ تَدِلُّ بِهِنَّ: إِنَّ جَدِّي وَجَدُّكَ وَاحِدٌ، وَإِنِّي أَنْكَحَنِيكَ اللَّهُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، وَإِنَّ السَّفِيرَ جِبْرِيلُ عليه السلام. 

وقوله: ﴿لِكَيْ لَا يَكُونَ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ حَرَجٌ فِي أَزْوَاجِ أَدْعِيَائِهِمْ إِذَا قَضَوْا مِنْهُنَّ وَطَرًا﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا أَبَحْنَا لَكَ تَزْوِيجَهَا وَفَعَلْنَا ذَلِكَ؛ لِئَلَّا يَبْقَى حَرَجٌ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فِي تَزْوِيجِ مُطَلَّقَاتِ الْأَدْعِيَاءِ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم كَانَ قَبْلَ النُّبُوَّةِ قَدْ تَبَنَّى زَيْدَ بْنَ حَارِثَةَ، فَكَانَ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "زَيْدُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ"، فَلَمَّا قَطَعَ اللَّهُ هَذِهِ النِّسْبَةَ بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا جَعَلَ أَدْعِيَاءَكُمْ أَبْنَاءَكُمْ ذَلِكُمْ قَوْلُكُمْ بِأَفْوَاهِكُمْ وَاللَّهُ يَقُولُ الْحَقَّ وَهُوَ يَهْدِي السَّبِيلَ ادْعُوهُمْ لآبَائِهِمْ هُوَ أَقْسَطُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ﴾ ، ثُمَّ زَادَ ذَلِكَ بَيَانًا وَتَأْكِيدًا بِوُقُوعِ تَزْوِيجِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِزَيْنَبَ بِنْتِ جَحْشٍ لَمَّا طَلَّقَهَا زَيْدُ بْنُ حَارِثَةَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ في آية التحريم: ﴿وَحَلائِلُ أَبْنَائِكُمُ الَّذِينَ مِنْ أَصْلابِكُم﴾ [النِّسَاءِ:٢٣] لِيَحْتَرِزَ مِنَ الِابْنِ الدَّعِي؛ فَإِنَّ ذَلِكَ كَانَ كَثِيرًا فِيهِمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَانَ أَمْرُ اللَّهِ مَفْعُولا﴾ أَيْ: وَكَانَ هَذَا الْأَمْرُ الَّذِي وَقَعَ قَدْ قَدَّرَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى وحَتَّمه، وَهُوَ كَائِنٌ لَا مَحَالَةَ، كَانَتْ زَيْنَبُ فِي عِلْمِ اللَّهِ سَتَصِيرُ مِنْ أَزْوَاجِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ.

---

## 33:38 — verse 38

### Translation

The Most High says: {There is no blame upon the Prophet concerning that which God has made obligatory for him}, meaning: concerning that which He made lawful for him and commanded him to do regarding his marrying Zaynab, whom his adopted son Zayd ibn Harithah had divorced.

His saying: {the way of God with those who passed before}, meaning: this is God's ruling concerning the prophets before him. He would not command them to do something and then hold it against them as blame. This is a refutation of those among the hypocrites who imagined there to be some deficiency in his marrying the wife of Zayd, his freedman and adopted son whom he had taken as a son.

{And the command of God is a decree destined to occur}, meaning: His command, which He decrees, inevitably comes to pass, occurring with no deviation from it and no way around it. So whatever [God] wills happens, and whatever He does not will does not happen.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَا كَانَ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ مِنْ حَرَجٍ فِيمَا فَرَضَ اللَّهُ لَهُ﴾ أَيْ: فِيمَا أَحَلَّ لَهُ وَأَمَرَهُ بِهِ مِنْ تَزْوِيجِ زَيْنَبَ الَّتِي طَلَّقَهَا دَعِيُّه زَيْدُ بْنُ حَارِثَةَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿سُنَّةَ اللَّهِ فِي الَّذِينَ خَلَوْا مِنْ قَبْلُ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا حُكْمُ اللَّهِ فِي الْأَنْبِيَاءِ قَبْلَهُ، لَمْ يَكُنْ لِيَأْمُرَهُمْ بِشَيْءٍ وَعَلَيْهِمْ فِي ذَلِكَ حَرج، وَهَذَا رَدٌّ عَلَى مَنْ تَوَهَّم مِن الْمُنَافِقِينَ نَقْصًا فِي تَزْوِيجِهِ امْرَأَةَ زَيْدٍ مَوْلَاهُ ودَعيه، الَّذِي كَانَ قَدْ تَبَنَّاهُ.

﴿وَكَانَ أَمْرُ اللَّهِ قَدَرًا مَقْدُورًا﴾ أَيْ: وَكَانَ أَمْرُهُ الَّذِي يقدِّره كَائِنًا لَا مَحَالَةَ، وَوَاقِعًا لَا مَحِيدَ عَنْهُ وَلَا مَعْدَلَ، فَمَا شَاءَ [اللَّهُ] كَانَ، وَمَا لَمْ يَشَأْ لَمْ يَكُنْ.

---

## 33:39-40 — verses 39-40 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted praises: {Those who convey the messages of Allah}, meaning to His creation, and discharge them with trustworthiness, {and fear Him}, meaning they fear Him and fear no one besides Him, so that no one's power or dominance prevents them from conveying the messages of Allah. {And sufficient is Allah as a reckoner}, meaning sufficient is Allah as a helper and supporter. The master of mankind in this station, indeed in every station, is Muhammad, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. For he undertook the discharge of the message and its conveyance to the people of the east and the west, to all types of the children of Adam, and Allah made His word, His religion, and His law manifest over all religions and laws. Every prophet before him had been sent to his own people specifically, but he, may Allah's prayers be upon him, was sent to all of creation, their Arabs and their non-Arabs alike: {Say, O mankind, indeed I am the Messenger of Allah to you all} [al-A'raf: 158]. Then the station of conveyance was inherited from him by his community after him, and the highest among those who undertook it after him were his Companions, may Allah be pleased with them. They conveyed from him as he had commanded them, in all his sayings, his deeds, and his states, in his night and his day, in his residence and his travel, in his private and his public affairs. May Allah be pleased with them and may they be pleased with Him. Then each later generation inherited it from those before them, down to our time, so that by their light the rightly guided are guided, and upon their path the divinely aided proceed. We ask Allah, the Generous, the Bestower, to make us among their successors.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, may Allah be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Let none of you belittle himself, seeing a matter of Allah concerning which he ought to speak, yet not speaking of it. Allah will then say: What prevented you from speaking about it? He will say: My Lord, I feared the people. Allah will say: I am more deserving to be feared."

It was also narrated from Abd al-Razzaq, from al-Thawri, from Zubayd, from Amr ibn Murrah.

Ibn Majah narrated it from Abu Kurayb, from Abdullah ibn Numayr and Abu Mu'awiyah, both from al-A'mash, with the same content.

Regarding His saying: {Muhammad is not the father of any of your men}, the Exalted forbade that it be said afterward, "Zayd ibn Muhammad," meaning he was not his father, even though he had adopted him. For the Prophet ﷺ, had no surviving male child who lived to reach maturity. Al-Qasim, al-Tayyib, and al-Tahir were born to him from Khadijah, but they died in infancy. Ibrahim was born to him from Mariyah the Copt, and he too died as a nursing infant. He had four daughters from Khadijah: Zaynab, Ruqayyah, Umm Kulthum, and Fatimah, may Allah be pleased with them all. Three of them died during his lifetime, while Fatimah survived until she was afflicted by his loss ﷺ, and then she died six months after him.

Regarding His saying: {But he is the Messenger of Allah and the Seal of the Prophets, and Allah has full knowledge of all things}, this is like His saying: {Allah knows best where to place His message} [al-An'am: 124]. This verse is an explicit text that there is no prophet after him. And if there is no prophet after him, then all the more certainly, by an even stronger and more evident reasoning, there is no messenger after him, for the station of messengership is more specific than the station of prophethood. Every messenger is a prophet, but the reverse does not hold. To this effect, mutawatir (mass-transmitted) hadiths have come from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, through the reports of a group of the Companions.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] al-Tufayl ibn Ubayy ibn Ka'b, from his father, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "My likeness among the prophets is that of a man who built a house, making it beautiful and complete, but leaving in it the space for one brick, which he did not place. So people began to go around the building, admiring it, and saying: If only the place of this brick were completed! So I am, among the prophets, the place of that brick."

Al-Tirmidhi narrated it from Bundar, from Abu Amir al-Aqadi, with the same content, and said: Hasan sahih (good and authentic).

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Anas ibn Malik said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Messengership and prophethood have come to an end. There is no messenger after me, nor any prophet." He said: This was hard upon the people. He said: He said: "But there are al-mubashshirat (the glad tidings)." They said: O Messenger of Allah, what are al-mubashshirat? He said: "The vision of the righteous Muslim man, which is one of the parts of prophethood."

Al-Tirmidhi likewise narrated it from al-Hasan ibn Muhammad al-Za'farani, from Affan ibn Muslim, with the same content, and said: Sahih gharib (authentic, singular in its chain) from the hadith of al-Mukhtar ibn Fulful.

Another hadith: Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi said: [chain] Jabir ibn Abdullah said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "My likeness and the likeness of the prophets is that of a man who built a house, making it complete and beautiful, except for the space of one brick. Whoever entered it and looked at it would say: How beautiful it is, except for the place of this brick! So I am the place of that brick. The prophets, peace be upon them, have been sealed with me."

Al-Bukhari, Muslim, and al-Tirmidhi narrated it through various chains from Sulaym ibn Hayyan, with the same content. Al-Tirmidhi said: Sahih gharib from this route.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, may Allah be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "My likeness and the likeness of the prophets [before me] is that of a man who built a house and completed it except for one brick. Then I came and completed that brick." Muslim alone narrated it, from the report of al-A'mash, with the same content.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu al-Tufayl said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "There is no prophethood after me except al-mubashshirat." He said: It was asked: What are al-mubashshirat, O Messenger of Allah? He said: "The good vision," or he said, "the righteous vision."

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Hammam ibn Munabbih said: This is what Abu Hurayrah related to us. He said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "My likeness and the likeness of the prophets before me is that of a man who built houses, making them beautiful, complete, and pleasing, except for the space of one brick in one of its corners. So people began to go around it, admiring the building, and saying: If only you had placed a brick here, your building would be complete! The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: So I was that brick."

Both al-Bukhari and Muslim narrated it from the hadith of Abd al-Razzaq.

Another hadith, also from Abu Hurayrah: Imam Muslim said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, reported that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I have been given superiority over the prophets in six things: I have been given the comprehensive words, I have been aided by awe, the spoils of war have been made lawful for me, the earth has been made for me a means of purification and a place of prostration, I have been sent to all of creation entirely, and the prophets have been sealed with me."

Al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Majah narrated it from the hadith of Isma'il ibn Ja'far, and al-Tirmidhi said: Hasan sahih.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Sa'id al-Khudri said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "My likeness and the likeness of the prophets before me is that of a man who built a house and completed it except for the space of one brick. Then I came and completed that brick."

Muslim narrated it from Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shaybah and Abu Kurayb, both from Abu Mu'awiyah, with the same content.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] al-Irbad ibn Sariyah said: The Prophet ﷺ said: "Indeed, with Allah I am already the Seal of the Prophets, while Adam is still being formed from his clay."

Another hadith: al-Zuhri said: Muhammad ibn Jubayr ibn Mut'im informed me, from his father, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "I have names: I am Muhammad, and I am Ahmad, and I am al-Mahi (the Effacer) by whom Allah effaces disbelief, and I am al-Hashir (the Gatherer) at whose feet mankind will be gathered, and I am al-Aqib (the Successor) after whom there is no prophet." Both Bukhari and Muslim narrated it in their Sahihs.

Imam Ahmad said: Yahya ibn Ishaq narrated to us, Ibn Lahi'ah narrated to us, from Abdullah ibn Hubayrah, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Jubayr, who said: I heard Abdullah ibn Amr say: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ came out to us one day like one bidding farewell, and said: "I am Muhammad, the unlettered Prophet," three times, "and there is no prophet after me. I have been given the openings of speech, its comprehensive totalities, and its conclusions. I know how many are the keepers of the Fire and the bearers of the Throne. I have been granted passage, and I have been spared, and my community has been spared. So listen and obey as long as I remain among you. When I am taken away, hold fast to the Book of Allah: make lawful what it makes lawful, and make unlawful what it makes unlawful." Imam Ahmad narrated this alone.

Ahmad also narrated it from Yahya ibn Ishaq, from Ibn Lahi'ah, from Abdullah ibn Hubayrah, from Abdullah ibn Marij al-Khawlani, from Abu Qays, the freed slave of Amr ibn al-As, from Abdullah ibn Amr, mentioning the same report exactly.

There are many hadiths on this subject. Among the mercy of Allah, Exalted is He, toward His servants is the sending of Muhammad ﷺ to them. Then, among the honor He bestowed upon them is the sealing of the prophets and messengers with him, and the completion of the upright religion through him. Allah, Exalted is He, has informed in His Book, and His Messenger has informed in the mutawatir (mass-transmitted) sunnah from him, that there is no prophet after him, so that people may know that anyone who claims this rank after him is a liar, a fabricator, a deceiver, misguided and misguiding, even if he performs feats of trickery and sleight of hand and produces various kinds of magic, talismans, and illusions. All of these are impossibilities and misguidance in the view of people of sound understanding, just as Allah, glorified and exalted is He, allowed to occur at the hands of al-Aswad al-Ansi in Yemen and Musaylimah the Liar in al-Yamamah: corrupt conditions and feeble utterances, which every person of intellect, understanding, and discernment knew to be the work of two liars who were astray. May Allah curse them both. So it is with every claimant of that rank until the Day of Resurrection, until they are sealed by the Masih al-Dajjal (the False Messiah). With each of these liars, Allah creates circumstances that bear witness, for the scholars and the believers, to the falsehood of whoever brings such claims. This is part of the completeness of Allah's kindness toward His creation, for such people, by the necessity of what actually occurs, do not enjoin what is right nor forbid what is wrong except by coincidence, or for purposes of their own directed toward something else, and they reach the utmost limit of falsehood and immorality in their sayings and their deeds, just as Allah, Exalted is He, said: {Shall I inform you upon whom the devils descend? They descend upon every sinful liar} [al-Shu'ara: 221-222], to the end of the verse. This is unlike the prophets (peace be upon them), for they are at the utmost limit of piety, truthfulness, right guidance, uprightness, and justice in what they say, what they do, what they command, and what they forbid, along with the extraordinary, custom-breaking signs, clear proofs, and dazzling demonstrations with which they are supported. So may the blessings and peace of Allah be upon them continuously and unceasingly, as long as the earth and the heavens endure.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَمْدَحُ تَعَالَى : ﴿الَّذِينَ يُبَلِّغُونَ رِسَالاتِ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: إِلَى خَلْقِهِ وَيُؤَدُّونَهَا بِأَمَانَتِهَا ﴿وَيَخْشَوْنَهُ﴾ أَيْ: يَخَافُونَهُ وَلَا يَخَافُونَ أَحَدًا سِوَاهُ فَلَا تَمْنَعُهُمْ سَطْوَةُ أَحَدٍ عَنْ إِبْلَاغِ رِسَالَاتِ اللَّهِ، ﴿وَكَفَى بِاللَّهِ حَسِيبًا﴾ أَيْ: وَكَفَى بِاللَّهِ نَاصِرًا وَمُعِينًا. وَسَيِّدُ النَّاسِ فِي هَذَا الْمَقَامِ -بَلْ وَفِي كُلِّ مَقَامٍ -مُحَمَّدٍ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ؛ فَإِنَّهُ قَامَ بِأَدَاءِ الرِّسَالَةِ وَإِبْلَاغِهَا إِلَى أَهْلِ الْمَشَارِقِ وَالْمَغَارِبِ، إِلَى جَمِيعِ أَنْوَاعِ بَنِي آدَمَ، وَأَظْهَرَ اللَّهُ كَلِمَتَهُ وَدِينَهُ وَشَرْعَهُ عَلَى جَمِيعِ الْأَدْيَانِ وَالشَّرَائِعِ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ كَانَ النَّبِيُّ يُبْعَثُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ خَاصَّةً، وَأَمَّا هُوَ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ، فَإِنَّهُ بُعث إِلَى جَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ عَرَبهم وَعَجَمِهِمْ، ﴿قُلْ يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ إِنِّي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِلَيْكُمْ جَمِيعًا﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٥٨] ، ثُمَّ وَرِثَ مَقَامَ الْبَلَاغِ عَنْهُ أُمَّتُهُ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ، فَكَانَ أَعْلَى مَنْ قَامَ بِهَا بَعْدَهُ أَصْحَابُهُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ، بَلَّغُوا عَنْهُ كَمَا أَمَرَهُمْ بِهِ فِي جَمِيعِ أَقْوَالِهِ وَأَفْعَالِهِ وَأَحْوَالِهِ، فِي لَيْلِهِ وَنَهَارِهِ، وحَضَره وَسَفَرِهِ، وَسِرِّهِ وَعَلَانِيَتِهِ، فَرَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ وَأَرْضَاهُمْ. ثُمَّ وَرِثَهُ كُلُّ خَلَفٍ عَنْ سَلَفِهِمْ إِلَى زَمَانِنَا هَذَا، فَبِنُورِهِمْ يَقْتَدِي الْمُهْتَدُونَ، وَعَلَى مَنْهَجِهِمْ يَسْلُكُ الْمُوَفَّقُونَ. فَنَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ الْكَرِيمَ الْمَنَّانَ أَنْ يَجْعَلَنَا مِنْ خَلَفِهِمْ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ نُمَيْر، أَخْبَرَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرَّة، عَنْ أَبِي البَخْتَري، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا يَحْقِرَنَّ أَحَدُكُمْ نَفْسَهُ أَنْ يَرَى أَمْرَ اللَّهِ فِيهِ مَقَالٌ ثُمَّ لَا يَقُولُهُ، فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ: مَا يَمْنَعُكَ أَنْ تَقُولَ فِيهِ؟ فَيَقُولُ: رَبِّ، خَشِيتُ النَّاسَ. فَيَقُولُ: فَأَنَا أَحَقُّ أن يخشى ".

وَرَوَاهُ أَيْضًا عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنِ الثَّوْرِيِّ، عَنْ زُبَيْدٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرَّةَ .

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، عَنِ أَبِي كُرَيْب، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ نُمَيْرٍ وَأَبِي مُعَاوِيَةَ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، بِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَا كَانَ مُحَمَّدٌ أَبَا أَحَدٍ مِنْ رِجَالِكُمْ﴾ ، نَهَى [تَعَالَى] أَنَّ يُقَالَ بَعْدَ هَذَا: "زَيْدُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ" أَيْ: لَمْ يَكُنْ أَبَاهُ وَإِنْ كَانَ قَدْ تَبَنَّاهُ، فَإِنَّهُ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَامُهُ، لَمْ يَعِشْ لَهُ وَلَدٌ ذَكَرٌ حَتَّى بَلَغَ الْحُلُمَ؛ فَإِنَّهُ وُلِدَ لَهُ الْقَاسِمُ، وَالطَّيِّبُ، وَالطَّاهِرُ، مِنْ خَدِيجَةَ فَمَاتُوا صِغَارًا، وَوُلِدَ لَهُ إِبْرَاهِيمُ مِنْ مَارِيَةَ الْقِبْطِيَّةِ، فَمَاتَ أَيْضًا رَضِيعًا ، وَكَانَ لَهُ مِنْ خَدِيجَةَ أَرْبَعُ بَنَاتٍ: زَيْنَبُ، وَرُقَيَّةُ، وَأُمُّ كُلْثُومٍ، وَفَاطِمَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ، فَمَاتَ فِي حَيَاتِهِ ثَلَاثٌ وَتَأَخَّرَتْ فَاطِمَةُ حَتَّى أُصِيبَتْ بِهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، ثُمَّ مَاتَتْ بَعْدَهُ لِسِتَّةِ أَشْهُرٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَكِنْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ وَخَاتَمَ النَّبِيِّينَ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمًا﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ حَيْثُ يَجْعَلُ رِسَالَتَهُ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:١٢٤] فَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ نَصٌّ فِي أَنَّهُ لَا نَبِيَّ بَعْدَهُ، وَإِذَا كَانَ لَا نَبِيَّ بَعْدَهُ فَلَا رَسُولَ [بَعْدَهُ] بِطَرِيقِ الْأَوْلَى وَالْأَحْرَى؛ لِأَنَّ مَقَامَ الرِّسَالَةِ أَخَصُّ مِنْ مَقَامِ النُّبُوَّةِ، فَإِنَّ كُلَّ رَسُولٍ نَبِيٌّ، وَلَا يَنْعَكِسُ. وَبِذَلِكَ وَرَدَتِ الْأَحَادِيثُ الْمُتَوَاتِرَةُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ من حَدِيثِ جَمَاعَةٍ مِنَ الصَّحَابَةِ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَامِرٍ الْأَزْدِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا زُهَيْر بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَقِيلٍ، عَنِ الطُّفَيْلِ بْنِ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَثَلِي فِي النَّبِيِّينَ كَمَثَلِ رَجُلٍ بَنَى دَارًا فَأَحْسَنَهَا وَأَكْمَلَهَا، وَتَرَكَ فِيهَا مَوْضِعَ لَبنة لَمْ يَضَعها، فَجَعَلَ النَّاسُ يَطُوفُونَ بِالْبُنْيَانِ وَيَعْجَبُونَ مِنْهُ، وَيَقُولُونَ: لَوْ تمَّ مَوْضِعُ هَذِهِ اللَّبِنَةِ؟ فَأَنَا فِي النَّبِيِّينَ مَوْضِعُ تِلْكَ اللَّبِنَةِ".

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، عَنْ بُنْدَار، عَنْ أَبِي عَامِرٍ الْعَقَدِيِّ، بِهِ ، وَقَالَ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْوَاحِدِ بْنُ زِيَادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُخْتَارُ بْنُ فُلفُل، حَدَّثَنَا أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنِ الرِّسَالَةَ وَالنُّبُوَّةَ قَدِ انْقَطَعَتْ، فَلَا رَسُولَ بَعْدِي وَلَا نَبِيَّ." قَالَ: فشَقّ ذَلِكَ عَلَى النَّاسِ قَالَ: قَالَ : وَلَكِنَّ الْمُبَشِّرَاتِ". قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، وَمَا الْمُبَشِّرَاتُ؟ قَالَ: "رُؤْيَا الرَّجُلِ الْمُسْلِمِ، وَهِيَ جُزْءٌ مِنْ أَجْزَاءِ النُّبُوَّةِ".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَى التِّرْمِذِيُّ عَنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ الزَّعْفَرَانِيِّ، عَنْ عَفَّانَ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، بِهِ وَقَالَ: صَحِيحٌ غَرِيبٌ مِنْ حديث المختار بن فُلفُل.

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا سَليم بْنُ حَيَّان، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ مِينَاءَ، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَثَلِي وَمَثَلُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ كَمَثَلِ رَجُلٍ بَنَى دَارًا فَأَكْمَلَهَا وَأَحْسَنَهَا إِلَّا مَوْضِعَ لَبنة، فَكَانَ مَنْ دَخَلَهَا فَنَظَرَ إِلَيْهَا قَالَ: مَا أَحْسَنَهَا إِلَّا مَوْضِعَ هَذِهِ اللَّبِنَةِ! فَأَنَا مَوْضِعُ اللَّبِنَةِ، خُتِمَ بِي الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ".

وَرَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ، وَمُسْلِمٌ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ سُلَيْمِ بْنِ حَيَّانَ، بِهِ. وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: صَحِيحٌ غَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ.

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: مَثَلِي وَمَثَلُ النَّبِيِّينَ [مِنْ قَبْلِي] كَمَثَلِ رَجُلٍ بَنَى دَارًا فَأَتَمَّهَا إِلَّا لَبنَة وَاحِدَةً، فَجِئْتُ أَنَا فَأَتْمَمْتُ تِلْكَ اللَّبِنَةِ". انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ مُسْلِمٌ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ الْأَعْمَشِ، بِهِ .

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ [الْإِمَامُ] أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ عُبَيد الرَّاسِبِيُّ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا الطُّفَيْلِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم: "لا نُبُوَّةَ بَعْدِي إِلَّا الْمُبَشِّرَاتِ". قَالَ: قِيلَ: وَمَا الْمُبَشِّرَاتُ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "الرُّؤْيَا الْحَسَنَةُ -أَوْ قَالَ -الرُّؤْيَا الصَّالِحَةُ." 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنْ هَمَّام بْنِ مُنَبِّه قَالَ: هَذَا مَا حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ مَثَلِي وَمَثَلَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ مِنْ قَبْلِي كَمَثَلِ رَجُلٍ ابْتَنَى بُيُوتًا فَأَحْسَنَهَا وَأَكْمَلَهَا وَأَجْمَلَهَا، إِلَّا مَوْضِعَ لَبنة مِنْ زَاوِيَةٍ مِنْ زَوَايَاهَا، فَجَعَلَ النَّاسُ يَطُوفُونَ وَيُعْجِبُهُمُ الْبُنْيَانُ وَيَقُولُونَ: أَلَا وَضَعْتَ هَاهُنَا لَبِنَةً فَيَتِمُّ بُنْيَانُكَ؟! " قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "فَكُنْتُ أَنَا اللَّبِنَةُ".

أَخْرَجَاهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّزَّاقِ. 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ أَيْضًا: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ مُسْلِمٌ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَيُّوبَ وَقُتَيْبَةُ وَعَلِيُّ بْنُ حَجَرٍ قَالُوا: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ جَعْفَرٍ، عَنِ الْعَلَاءِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم قال: "فُضلت عَلَى الْأَنْبِيَاءِ بِسِتٍّ: أعْطِيتُ جَوَامِعَ الْكَلِمِ، ونُصِرْتُ بِالرُّعْبِ، وأحِلَّت لِيَ الْغَنَائِمُ، وَجُعِلَتْ لِيَ الْأَرْضُ طَهُورًا وَمَسْجِدًا، وَأُرْسِلْتُ إِلَى الْخَلْقِ كَافَّةً، وختم بي النبيون".

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ جَعْفَرٍ، وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ. 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَثَلِي وَمَثَلُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ مِنْ قَبْلِي، كَمَثَلِ رَجُلٍ بَنَى دَارًا فَأَتَمَّهَا إِلَّا مَوْضِعَ لَبِنَةٍ وَاحِدَةٍ، فَجِئْتُ أَنَا فَأَتْمَمْتُ تِلْكَ اللَّبِنَةَ".

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، وَأَبِي كُرَيْب، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ أَبِي مُعَاوِيَةَ، بِهِ. 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مَهْدِيٍّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ صَالِحٍ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ سُويد الْكَلْبِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى بْنِ هِلَالٍ السُّلَمِيِّ، عَنِ العِرْباض بْنِ سَارِيَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "إِنِّي عِنْدَ اللَّهِ لَخَاتَمُ النَّبِيِّينَ وَإِنَّ آدَمَ لمنْجَدِل فِي طِينَتِهِ." 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الزُّهْرِيُّ: أَخْبَرَنِي مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرِ بْنِ مُطْعِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ لِي أَسْمَاءٌ: أَنَا مُحَمَّدٌ، وَأَنَا أَحْمَدُ، وَأَنَا الْمَاحِي الَّذِي يَمْحُو اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بِيَ الْكُفْرَ، وَأَنَا الْحَاشِرُ الَّذِي يُحْشَرُ النَّاسُ عَلَى قَدَمِي، وَأَنَا الْعَاقِبُ الَّذِي لَيْسَ بَعْدَهُ نَبِيٌّ." أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ هُبَيْرة، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عَمْرٍو يَقُولُ: خَرَجَ عَلَيْنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَوْمًا كَالْمُوَدِّعِ، فَقَالَ: "أَنَا مُحَمَّدٌ النَّبِيُّ الْأُمِّيُّ -ثَلَاثًا -وَلَا نَبِيَّ بَعْدِي، أُوتِيتُ فَوَاتِحَ الْكَلِمِ وَجَوَامِعَهُ وَخَوَاتِمَهُ، وَعَلِمْتُ كَمْ خَزَنَةُ النَّارِ وَحَمَلَةُ الْعَرْشِ، وَتُجُوِّزَ بِي، وعُوفيتُ وعُوفيتْ أُمَّتِي؛ فَاسْمَعُوا وَأَطِيعُوا مَا دُمْتُ فِيكُمْ، فَإِذَا ذُهب بِي فَعَلَيْكُمْ بِكِتَابِ اللَّهِ، أَحِلُّوا حَلَالَهُ، وَحَرِّمُوا حَرَامَهُ". تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ. 

وَرَوَاهُ [الْإِمَامُ] أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ ابْنُ لَهِيعة، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ هُبَيْرَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَرِيجٍ الْخَوْلَانِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي قَيْسٍ -مَوْلَى عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ -عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو فَذَكَرَ مِثْلَهُ سَوَاءً .

وَالْأَحَادِيثُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ، فَمِنْ رَحْمَةِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى بِالْعِبَادِ إِرْسَالُ مُحَمَّدٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، إِلَيْهِمْ، ثُمَّ مِنْ تَشْرِيفِهِ لَهُمْ خَتْمُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ وَالْمُرْسَلِينَ بِهِ، وَإِكْمَالُ الدِّينِ الْحَنِيفِ لَهُ. وَقَدْ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى فِي كِتَابِهِ، وَرَسُولِهِ فِي السُّنَّةِ الْمُتَوَاتِرَةِ عَنْهُ: أَنَّهُ لَا نَبِيَّ بَعْدَهُ؛ لِيَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ كُلَّ مَنِ ادعى هذا المقام بعده فَهُوَ كَذَّابٌ أَفَّاكٌ، دَجَّالٌ ضَالٌّ مُضِلٌّ، وَلَوْ تَخَرَّقَ وَشَعْبَذَ، وَأَتَى بِأَنْوَاعِ السِّحْرِ وَالطَّلَاسِمِ والنَيرجيَّات ، فَكُلُّهَا مُحَالٌ وَضَلَالٌ عِنْدَ أُولِي الْأَلْبَابِ، كَمَا أَجْرَى اللَّهُ، سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى، عَلَى يَدِ الْأَسْوَدِ العَنْسي بِالْيَمَنِ، وَمُسَيْلِمَةَ الْكَذَّابِ بِالْيَمَامَةِ، مِنَ الْأَحْوَالِ الْفَاسِدَةِ وَالْأَقْوَالِ الْبَارِدَةِ، مَا عَلِمَ كُلُّ ذِي لُبٍّ وَفَهْمٍ وحِجى أَنَّهُمَا كَاذِبَانِ ضَالَّانِ، لَعَنَهُمَا اللَّهُ. وَكَذَلِكَ كُلُّ مُدَّعٍ لِذَلِكَ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ حَتَّى يُخْتَمُوا بِالْمَسِيحِ الدَّجَّالِ، [فَكُلُّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْ هَؤُلَاءِ الْكَذَّابِينَ] يَخْلُقُ اللَّهُ مَعَهُ مِنَ الْأُمُورِ مَا يَشْهَدُ الْعُلَمَاءُ وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ بِكَذِبِ مَنْ جَاءَ بِهَا. وَهَذَا مِنْ تَمَامِ لُطْفِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى بِخَلْقِهِ، فَإِنَّهُمْ بِضَرُورَةِ الْوَاقِعِ لَا يَأْمُرُونَ بِمَعْرُوفٍ وَلَا يَنْهَوْنَ عَنْ مُنْكَرٍ إِلَّا عَلَى سَبِيلِ الِاتِّفَاقِ، أَوْ لِمَا لَهُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الْمَقَاصِدِ إِلَى غَيْرِهِ، وَيَكُونُ فِي غَايَةِ الْإِفْكِ وَالْفُجُورِ فِي أَقْوَالِهِمْ وَأَفْعَالِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هَلْ أُنَبِّئُكُمْ عَلَى مَنْ تَنزلُ الشَّيَاطِينُ * تَنزلُ عَلَى كُلِّ أَفَّاكٍ أَثِيمٍ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الشُّعَرَاءِ:٢٢١، ٢٢٢] . وَهَذَا بِخِلَافِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ، فَإِنَّهُمْ فِي غَايَةِ الْبِرِّ وَالصِّدْقِ وَالرُّشْدِ وَالِاسْتِقَامَةِ [وَالْعَدْلِ] فِيمَا يَقُولُونَهُ وَيَفْعَلُونَهُ وَيَأْمُرُونَ بِهِ وَيَنْهَوْنَ عَنْهُ، مَعَ مَا يُؤَيِّدُونَ بِهِ مِنَ الْخَوَارِقِ لِلْعَادَاتِ، وَالْأَدِلَّةِ الْوَاضِحَاتِ، وَالْبَرَاهِينِ الْبَاهِرَاتِ، فَصَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمْ دَائِمًا مستمرا ما دامت الأرض والسموات.

---

## 33:41-44 — verses 41-44 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, commanding His believing servants to make abundant remembrance of their Lord, the Exalted, who has bestowed upon them varieties of blessings and kinds of favors, because of the abundant reward and the beautiful return that they have in that.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu al-Darda', may Allah be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Shall I not tell you of the best of your deeds, the purest of them before your Sovereign, the most elevated of them in your ranks, better for you than giving gold and silver, and better for you than meeting your enemy so that you strike their necks and they strike yours?" They said: "What is it, O Messenger of Allah?" He said: "The remembrance of Allah, Mighty and Majestic."

Thus it was narrated by al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Majah, from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Sa'id ibn Abi Hind, from Ziyad, the mawla (client) of Ibn Ayyash, from Abu Bahriyyah, whose name was Abdullah ibn Qays al-Taraghimi, from Abu al-Darda', with it. Al-Tirmidhi said: Some of them narrated it from him and made it mursal (with a missing link at the end).

I say: this hadith has already been mentioned at His saying, {and the men who remember Allah much and the women who remember}, in the Musnad of [Imam] Ahmad, from the hadith of Ziyad ibn Abi Ziyad, mawla of Abdullah ibn Ayyash, that it reached him from Mu'adh ibn Jabal, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, similarly. And Allah knows best.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah said: "A supplication I heard from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ which I do not abandon: 'O Allah, make me magnify Your gratitude, follow Your counsel, make abundant Your remembrance, and preserve Your commandment.'"

Al-Tirmidhi narrated it from Yahya ibn Musa, from Waki', from Abu Fadalah al-Faraj ibn Fadalah, from Abu Sa'id al-Himsi, from Abu Hurayrah, mentioning the same, and said: gharib (singular).

Thus Imam Ahmad also narrated it from Abu al-Nadr Hashim ibn al-Qasim, from Faraj ibn Fadalah, from Abu Sa'id al-Madani, from Abu Hurayrah, and mentioned it.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abdullah ibn Busr said: Two bedouins came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. One of them said: "O Messenger of Allah, who among people is best?" He said: "He whose life is long and whose deeds are good." The other said: "O Messenger of Allah, the laws of Islam have become numerous for us, so instruct me in something I may hold fast to." He said: "Let your tongue remain moist with the remembrance of Allah."

Al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Majah narrated the second part of it from the hadith of Mu'awiyah ibn Salih, with it. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan gharib (good, singular).

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Sa'id al-Khudri reported that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Make abundant remembrance of Allah until they say: he is mad."

Al-Tabarani said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Remember Allah with abundant remembrance, until the hypocrites say: they are showing off."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abdullah ibn Amr said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "No people sit in a gathering in which they do not remember Allah, except that they will see it as a cause of regret on the Day of Resurrection."

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying, {Remember Allah with abundant remembrance}: Allah did not impose any obligation upon His servants except that He set for it a known limit, then excused its people in a state of excuse, except remembrance, for Allah did not set for it a limit at which it ends, nor did He excuse anyone from abandoning it, except one overcome in abandoning it. He said: {So remember Allah, standing, sitting, and on your sides} [al-Nisa: 103], by night and by day, on land and sea, while traveling and while at home, in wealth and in poverty, in health and in sickness, secretly and openly, and in every state. And He said: {And glorify Him morning and evening}. So when you do that, He and His angels send blessings upon you.

The hadiths, verses, and reports urging remembrance of Allah are very numerous, and in this noble verse is an urging to make it abundant.

People have composed works on the remembrances associated with the hours of night and day, such as al-Nasa'i, al-Ma'mari, and others. Among the best books composed on that subject is the Book of Remembrances by Shaykh Muhyi al-Din al-Nawawi, may Allah the Exalted have mercy on him. His saying, {And glorify Him morning and evening} means at morning and evening, as in His saying: {So glory be to Allah when you reach evening and when you reach morning. And to Him is praise in the heavens and the earth, and at afternoon and when you reach midday} [al-Rum: 17-18].

His saying, {He it is who sends blessings upon you, and His angels}: this is an incitement to remembrance, meaning that He, glory be to Him, remembers you, so remember Him yourselves, as in His saying: {As We have sent among you a messenger from yourselves, reciting to you Our verses, purifying you, and teaching you the Book and wisdom, and teaching you what you did not know. So remember Me, I will remember you, and be grateful to Me and do not be ungrateful to Me} [al-Baqarah: 151-152]. And the Prophet ﷺ said: "Allah says: whoever remembers Me within himself, I remember him within Myself, and whoever remembers Me in an assembly, I remember him in an assembly better than them."

Blessing (salah) from Allah is His praise of the servant before the angels. Al-Bukhari related this from Abu al-Aliyah. Abu Ja'far al-Razi narrated it from al-Rabi' ibn Anas, from him.

Others said: blessing from Allah is mercy, and this was countered by His saying, {upon those are blessings from their Lord and mercy}.

It may be said that there is no contradiction between the two sayings. And Allah knows best.

As for the blessing (salah) from the angels, it is in the sense of supplication for people and asking forgiveness for them, as in His saying: {Those who bear the Throne and those around it glorify their Lord with praise and believe in Him and ask forgiveness for those who have believed: Our Lord, You embrace all things in mercy and knowledge, so forgive those who repent and follow Your path, and protect them from the punishment of the Blazing Fire. Our Lord, admit them into the Gardens of Eden which You have promised them, and whoever was righteous among their fathers, their spouses, and their descendants. Indeed, You are the Almighty, the Wise. And protect them from evils} [Ghafir: 7-9].

His saying, {that He may bring you out of darkness into light}, means: because of His mercy toward you, His praise of you, and the supplication of His angels for you, He brings you out of the darknesses of ignorance and misguidance into the light of guidance and certainty. {And He is ever Merciful to the believers}, meaning in this world and the next. As for in this world: He guided them to the truth of which others were ignorant, and made clear to them the path from which others among the callers to disbelief or innovation and their rabble of followers strayed and turned away. As for His mercy toward them in the next life: He secured them from the greatest terror, and commanded His angels to receive them with the glad tidings of attaining Paradise and salvation from the Fire, and that was only because of His love for them and His compassion toward them.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Anas, may Allah be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ passed by with a group of his companions, and there was a child in the road. When his mother saw the people, she feared for her child that he would be trampled, so she came running, saying, "My son, my son," and hastened and took him. The people said: "O Messenger of Allah, would this woman ever throw her son into the fire?" He said, calming them, and said: "Nor would Allah, He will not throw His beloved into the Fire."

Its chain meets the standard of the two Sahihs, though none of the authors of the Six Books recorded it. But in the Sahih of Imam al-Bukhari, from the Commander of the Faithful, Umar ibn al-Khattab, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ saw a woman among the captives who had taken a child of hers, pressed it to her chest, and nursed it. He said: "Do you think this woman would throw her child into the fire while she has the power to prevent it?" They said: "No." He said: "By Allah, Allah is more merciful to His servants than this woman is to her child."

His saying, {Their greeting on the day they meet Him will be 'Peace'}: the apparent meaning, and Allah knows best, is that {their greeting}, that is, from Allah the Exalted, on the day they meet Him, {will be 'Peace'}, meaning on the day He greets them with peace, as He said: {Peace, a word from a Merciful Lord} [Ya-Sin: 58].

Qatadah claimed that what is meant is that they will greet one another with peace on the day they meet Allah in the Hereafter. Ibn Jarir preferred this view.

I say: support may be found for this in His saying, {Their call therein will be 'Glory be to You, O Allah,' and their greeting therein will be 'Peace,' and the last of their call will be 'Praise be to Allah, Lord of the worlds'} [Yunus: 10].

His saying, {and He has prepared for them a generous reward}, means Paradise and what is in it of foods, drinks, garments, dwellings, marriages, pleasures, and sights, and what no eye has seen, no ear has heard, and what has never occurred to the heart of any human being.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى آمِرًا عِبَادَهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِكَثْرَةِ ذِكْرِهِمْ لِرَبِّهِمْ تَعَالَى، الْمُنْعِمِ عَلَيْهِمْ بِأَنْوَاعِ النِّعَمِ وَأَصْنَافِ الْمِنَنِ، لِمَا لَهُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ مِنْ جَزِيلِ الثَّوَابِ، وَجَمِيلِ الْمَآبِ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بن سعيد ، حدثني مولى بن عَيَّاشٍ عَنْ أَبِي بَحرية ، عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَلَّا أُنْبِئَكُمْ بِخَيْرِ أعمالكم وأزكاها عند مليككم، وأرفعها في درجاتكم، وَخَيْرٍ لَكُمْ مِنْ إِعْطَاءِ الذَّهَبِ والوَرق، وَخَيْرٍ لَكُمْ مِنْ أَنْ تَلْقَوْا عَدُوَّكُمْ فَتَضْرِبُوا أَعْنَاقَهُمْ، وَيَضْرِبُوا أَعْنَاقَكُمْ؟ " قَالُوا: وَمَا هُوَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "ذِكْرُ اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي هِنْدٍ، عَنْ زِيَادٍ -مَوْلَى ابْنِ عَيَّاشٍ -عَنْ أَبِي بَحرية -وَاسْمُهُ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ قَيْسٍ التَّرَاغِمِيُّ -عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ، بِهِ . قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: وَرَوَاهُ بَعْضُهُمْ عنه فأرسله.

قُلْتُ: وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالذَّاكِرِينَ اللَّهَ كَثِيرًا وَالذَّاكِرَاتِ﴾ فِي مُسْنَدِ [الْإِمَامِ] أَحْمَدَ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ زِيَادِ بْنِ أَبِي زِيَادٍ مَوْلَى عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَيَّاش: أَنَّهُ بَلَغَهُ عَنْ مُعَاذِ بْنِ جَبَلٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، بِنَحْوِهِ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا فَرَجُ بْنُ فَضَالة، عَنْ أَبِي سَعْدٍ الحِمْصي قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ يَقُولُ: دُعَاءٌ سَمِعْتَهُ مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَا أَدَعُهُ: "اللَّهُمَّ، اجْعَلْنِي أُعْظِمُ شُكْرَكَ، وَأَتْبَعُ نَصِيحَتَكَ، وَأُكْثِرُ ذِكْرَكَ، وَأَحْفَظُ وَصِيَّتَكَ". 

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ مُوسَى، عَنْ وَكِيعٍ، عَنْ أَبِي فَضَالَةَ الْفَرَجِ بْنِ فَضَالَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْحِمْصِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، فَذَكَرَ مِثْلَهُ وَقَالَ: غَرِيبٌ. 

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا عَنْ أَبِي النَّضْرِ هَاشِمِ بْنِ الْقَاسِمِ، عَنْ فَرَجِ بْنِ فَضَالَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْمَدَنِيِّ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ فَذَكَرَهُ. 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مَهْدِي، عَنْ مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ قَيْسٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ بُسْر يَقُولُ: جَاءَ أَعُرَابِيَّانِ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ أَحَدُهُمَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَيُّ النَّاسِ خَيْرٌ؟ قَالَ: "مَنْ طَالَ عُمْرُهُ وَحَسُنَ عَمَلُهُ". وَقَالَ الْآخَرُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّ شَرَائِعَ الْإِسْلَامِ قَدْ كَثُرَتْ عَلَيْنَا ، فَمُرْنِي بِأَمْرٍ أَتَشَبَّثُ بِهِ. قَالَ: "لَا يَزَالُ لِسَانُكَ رَطْبًا بِذِكْرِ اللَّهِ". 

وَرَوَى التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ [مِنْهُ] الْفَصْلَ الثَّانِي، مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ، بِهِ. وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُرَيج ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْحَارِثِ قَالَ: أَنَّ دَرّاجا أَبَا السَّمْحِ حَدَّثَهُ، عَنْ أَبِي الْهَيْثَمِ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "أَكْثِرُوا ذِكْرَ اللَّهِ حَتَّى يَقُولُوا: مَجْنُونٌ." 

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَحْمَدَ، حَدَّثَنَا عُقْبَةُ بْنُ مُكرم العَمِّي، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ سُفْيَانَ الجَحْدَرِي، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ أَبِي جَعْفَرٍ، عَنْ عُقْبَةَ بْنِ أَبِي ثُبَيت الرَّاسِبِيِّ، عَنِ أَبِي الْجَوْزَاءِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "اذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ ذِكْرًا كَثِيرًا [حَتَّى] يقول الْمُنَافِقُونَ: تُرَاءُونَ." 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ مَوْلَى بَنِي هَاشِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شَدَّادٌ أَبُو طَلْحَةَ الرَّاسِبِيُّ، سَمِعْتُ أَبَا الْوَازِعِ جَابِرَ بْنَ عَمْرٍو يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْ قَوْمٍ جَلَسُوا مَجْلِسًا لَمْ يَذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ فِيهِ، إِلَّا رَأَوْهُ حَسْرَةً يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ." 

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿اذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ ذِكْرًا كَثِيرًا﴾ : إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمْ يَفْرِضْ [عَلَى عِبَادِهِ] فَرِيضَةً إِلَّا [جَعَلَ لَهَا حَدًّا مَعْلُومًا، ثُمَّ] عَذَرَ أَهْلَهَا فِي حَالِ عُذْرٍ، غَيْرَ الذِّكْرِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمْ يَجْعَلْ لَهُ حَدًّا يَنْتَهِي إِلَيْهِ، وَلَمْ يَعْذُرْ أَحَدًا فِي تَرْكِهِ، إِلَّا مَغْلُوبًا عَلَى تَرْكِهِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿فَاذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ قِيَامًا وَقُعُودًا وَعَلَى جُنُوبِكُمْ﴾ [النِّسَاءِ:١٠٣] ، بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ، [فِي الْبَرِّ وَالْبَحْرِ] ، وَفِي السِّفْرِ وَالْحَضَرِ، وَالْغِنَى وَالْفَقْرِ، وَالصِّحَّةِ وَالسَّقَمِ، وَالسِّرِّ وَالْعَلَانِيَةِ، وَعَلَى كُلِّ حَالٍ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَسَبِّحُوهُ بُكْرَةً وَأَصِيلا﴾ فَإِذَا فَعَلْتُمْ ذَلِكَ صَلَّى عَلَيْكُمْ هُوَ وَمَلَائِكَتُهُ.

وَالْأَحَادِيثُ وَالْآيَاتُ وَالْآثَارُ فِي الْحَثِّ عَلَى ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ كَثِيرَةٌ جِدًّا، وَفِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ الْحَثُّ عَلَى الْإِكْثَارِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَدْ صَنَّفَ النَّاسُ فِي الْأَذْكَارِ الْمُتَعَلِّقَةِ بِآنَاءِ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ كَالنَّسَائِيِّ وَالْمَعْمَرِيِّ وَغَيْرِهِمَا ، وَمِنْ أَحْسَنِ الْكُتُبِ الْمُؤَلَّفَةِ فِي ذَلِكَ كِتَابُ الْأَذْكَارِ لِلشَّيْخِ مُحْيِي الدِّينِ النَّوَوِيِّ، رَحِمَهُ الله تعالى وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَسَبِّحُوهُ بُكْرَةً وَأَصِيلا﴾ أَيْ: عِنْدَ الصَّبَاحِ وَالْمَسَاءِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَسُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ حِينَ تُمْسُونَ وَحِينَ تُصْبِحُونَ وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَعَشِيًّا وَحِينَ تُظْهِرُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ:١٧، ١٨]

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿هُوَ الَّذِي يُصَلِّي عَلَيْكُمْ وَمَلائِكَتُهُ﴾ : هَذَا تَهْيِيجٌ إِلَى الذِّكْرِ، أَيْ: إِنَّهُ سُبْحَانَهُ يَذْكُرُكُمْ فَاذْكُرُوهُ أَنْتُمْ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا فِيكُمْ رَسُولا مِنْكُمْ يَتْلُو عَلَيْكُمْ آيَاتِنَا وَيُزَكِّيكُمْ وَيُعَلِّمُكُمُ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَيُعَلِّمُكُمْ مَا لَمْ تَكُونُوا تَعْلَمُونَ. فَاذْكُرُونِي أَذْكُرْكُمْ وَاشْكُرُوا لِي وَلا تَكْفُرُونِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٥١، ١٥٢] . وَقَالَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ: "يَقُولُ اللَّهُ: مَنْ ذَكَرَنِي فِي نَفْسِهِ ذَكَرْتُهُ فِي نَفْسِي، ومَنْ ذَكَرَنِي فِي مَلأ ذَكَرْتُهُ فِي مَلَأٍ خَيْرٍ مِنْهُمْ" 

وَالصَّلَاةُ مِنَ اللَّهِ ثَنَاؤُهُ عَلَى الْعَبْدِ عِنْدَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ، حَكَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ عَنْ أَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ. وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيُّ، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: الصَّلَاةُ مِنَ اللَّهِ: الرَّحْمَةُ [وَرَدَّ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ عَلَيْهِمْ صَلَوَاتٌ مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ وَرَحْمَةٌ﴾ ] 

وَقَدْ يُقَالُ: لَا مُنَافَاةَ بَيْنَ الْقَوْلَيْنِ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَأَمَّا الصَّلَاةُ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ، فَبِمَعْنَى الدُّعَاءِ لِلنَّاسِ وَالِاسْتِغْفَارِ ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿الَّذِينَ يَحْمِلُونَ الْعَرْشَ وَمَنْ حَوْلَهُ يُسَبِّحُونَ بِحَمْدِ رَبِّهِمْ وَيُؤْمِنُونَ بِهِ وَيَسْتَغْفِرُونَ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا رَبَّنَا وَسِعْتَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ رَحْمَةً وَعِلْمًا فَاغْفِرْ لِلَّذِينَ تَابُوا وَاتَّبَعُوا سَبِيلَكَ وَقِهِمْ عَذَابَ الْجَحِيمِ رَبَّنَا وَأَدْخِلْهُمْ جَنَّاتِ عَدْنٍ الَّتِي وَعَدْتَهُمْ وَمَنْ صَلَحَ مِنْ آبَائِهِمْ وَأَزْوَاجِهِمْ وَذُرِّيَّاتِهِمْ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ وَقِهِمُ السَّيِّئَاتِ﴾ الْآيَةَ. [غَافِرٍ: ٧-٩] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِيُخْرِجَكُمْ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ﴾ أَيْ: بِسَبَبِ رَحْمَتِهِ بِكُمْ وَثَنَائِهِ عَلَيْكُمْ، وَدُعَاءِ مَلَائِكَتِهِ لَكُمْ، يُخْرِجُكُمْ مِنْ ظُلُمَاتِ الْجَهْلِ وَالضَّلَالِ إِلَى نُورِ الْهُدَى وَالْيَقِينِ. ﴿وَكَانَ بِالْمُؤْمِنِينَ رَحِيمًا﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، أَمَّا فِي الدُّنْيَا: فَإِنَّهُ هَدَاهُمْ إِلَى الْحَقِّ الَّذِي جَهِلَهُ غَيْرُهُمْ، وبَصّرهم الطَّرِيقَ الَّذِي ضَلَّ عَنْهُ وَحَادَ عَنْهُ مِنْ سِوَاهُمْ مِنَ الدُّعَاةِ إِلَى الْكَفْرِ أَوِ الْبِدْعَةِ وَأَشْيَاعِهِمْ مِنَ الطَّغَامِ . وَأَمَّا رَحْمَتُهُ بِهِمْ فِي الْآخِرَةِ: فَآمَنَهُمْ مِنَ الْفَزَعِ الْأَكْبَرِ، وَأَمَرَ مَلَائِكَتَهُ يَتَلَقَّوْنَهُمْ بِالْبِشَارَةِ بِالْفَوْزِ بِالْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّجَاةِ مِنَ النَّارِ، وَمَا ذَاكَ إِلَّا لِمَحَبَّتِهِ لَهُمْ وَرَأْفَتِهِ بِهِمْ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ أَبِي عَدِيٍّ، عَنْ حُمَيْدٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: مَرَّ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي نَفَرٍ مِنْ أَصْحَابِهِ وَصَبِيٍّ فِي الطَّرِيقِ، فَلَمَّا رَأَتْ أُمُّهُ الْقَوْمَ خَشِيَتْ عَلَى وَلَدِهَا أَنْ يُوطَأَ، فَأَقْبَلَتْ تَسْعَى وَتَقُولُ: ابْنَيِ ابْنِي، وَسَعَت فَأَخَذَتْهُ، فَقَالَ الْقَوْمُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا كَانَتْ هَذِهِ لِتُلْقِيَ ابْنَهَا فِي النَّارِ. قَالَ: فَخَفَّضهم رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم وقال: "وَلَا اللَّهُ ، لَا يُلْقِي حَبِيبَهُ فِي النَّارِ".

إِسْنَادُهُ عَلَى شَرْطِ الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجْهُ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ الْكُتُبِ السِّتَّةِ ، وَلَكِنْ فِي صَحِيحِ الْإِمَامِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، عَنْ أَمِيرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ رَأَى امْرَأَةً مِنَ السَّبْيِ قَدْ أَخَذَتْ صَبِيًّا لَهَا، فَأَلْصَقَتْهُ إِلَى صَدْرِهَا، وَأَرْضَعَتْهُ فَقَالَ: "أَتَرَوْنَ هَذِهِ تُلْقِي وَلَدَهَا فِي النَّارِ وَهِيَ تَقْدِرُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ؟ " قَالُوا: لَا. قَالَ: "فَوَاللَّهِ، لَلَّهُ أَرْحَمُ بِعِبَادِهِ مِنْ هَذِهِ بِوَلَدِهَا" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿تَحِيَّتُهُمْ يَوْمَ يَلْقَوْنَهُ سَلامٌ﴾ الظَّاهِرُ أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ -وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ - ﴿تَحِيَّتُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى يَوْمَ يَلْقَوْنَهُ ﴿سَلامٌ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ يُسَلِّمُ عَلَيْهِمْ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿سَلامٌ قَوْلا مِنْ رَبٍّ رَحِيمٍ﴾ [يس:٥٨] .

وَزَعَمَ قَتَادَةُ أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ أَنَّهُمْ يُحَيِّي بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا بِالسَّلَامِ، يَوْمَ يَلْقَوْنَ اللَّهَ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

قُلْتُ: وَقَدْ يُسْتَدَلُّ بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿دَعْوَاهُمْ فِيهَا سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ وَتَحِيَّتُهُمْ فِيهَا سَلامٌ وَآخِرُ دَعْوَاهُمْ أَنِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ١٠] ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَعَدَّ لَهُمْ أَجْرًا كَرِيمًا﴾ يَعْنِي: الْجَنَّةَ وَمَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْمَآكِلِ وَالْمُشَارِبِ، وَالْمَلَابِسِ وَالْمَسَاكِنِ، وَالْمَنَاكَحِ وَالْمَلَاذِّ وَالْمَنَاظِرِ وَمَا لَا عَيْنٌ رَأَتْ، وَلَا أُذُنٌ سَمِعَتْ، وَلَا خَطَرَ عَلَى قَلْبِ بَشَرٍ.

---

## 33:45-48 — verses 45-48 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Imam Ahmad said: Musa ibn Dawud told us, Fulayh ibn Sulayman told us, from Hilal ibn Ali, from Ata' ibn Yasar, who said: I met Abdullah ibn Amr ibn al-As and said to him: Tell me about the description of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ in the Torah. He said: Yes indeed, by Allah, he is described in the Torah with the same description as in the Qur'an: {O Prophet, indeed We have sent you as a witness, a bearer of good tidings, and a warner} and as a fortress for the unlettered ones. You are My servant and My messenger, I have named you al-Mutawakkil (the one who relies utterly on Allah). You are not harsh nor coarse, nor one who raises his voice in the marketplaces, and he does not repel evil with evil but rather pardons and forgives. Allah will not take him until He establishes through him the crooked religion, by means of the testimony that there is no god but Allah, and thereby opens blind eyes, deaf ears, and covered hearts.

Al-Bukhari related it in "al-Buyu'" (Sales) from Muhammad ibn Sinan, from Fulayh ibn Sulayman, from Hilal ibn Ali, with this chain. He also related it in the Tafsir from Abdullah, said to be Ibn Raja', and said to be Ibn Salih, from Abd al-Aziz ibn Abi Salamah, from Hilal, from Ata' ibn Yasar, from Abdullah ibn Amr, with this chain. Ibn Abi Hatim related it from his father, from Abdullah ibn Raja', from Abd al-Aziz ibn Abi Salamah al-Majishun, with this chain.

Al-Bukhari said in "al-Buyu'": Sa'id said, from Hilal, from Ata', from Abdullah ibn Salam.

Wahb ibn Munabbih said: Allah revealed to a prophet among the prophets of the Children of Israel, called Sha'ya (Isaiah), saying: Stand among your people, the Children of Israel, for I shall give voice to your tongue through revelation, and I shall raise up an unlettered one from among the unlettered. I shall send him as [a bearer of good tidings], neither harsh nor coarse, nor one who raises his voice in the marketplaces. Were he to pass beside a lamp, he would not extinguish it, out of his tranquility, and were he to walk upon reeds, no sound would be heard beneath his feet. I shall send him as a bearer of good tidings and a warner. He does not speak obscenity. Through him I shall open blind eyes, deaf ears, and covered hearts. I shall guide him rightly to every fine matter, and grant him every noble character trait. I shall make tranquility his garment, righteousness his emblem, piety his innermost conscience, wisdom his speech, truthfulness and faithfulness his nature, pardon and kindness his character, truth his law, justice his conduct, guidance his leader, Islam his religion, and Ahmad his name. Through him I shall guide after misguidance, teach after ignorance, raise up after lowliness, make known after obscurity, multiply after scarcity, enrich after poverty, gather together after division, and unite through him nations that were scattered, hearts that were divided, and desires that were dispersed. Through him I shall rescue vast multitudes of people from ruin, and I shall make his community the best community brought forth for mankind, who enjoin what is right and forbid what is wrong, affirming the oneness of Allah, believing, sincere, confirming what My messengers brought. I shall inspire them with glorification, praise, exaltation, magnification, and the affirmation of Allah's oneness in their mosques, their gatherings, their resting places, their comings and goings, and their dwellings. They shall pray to Me standing and sitting, and fight in the path of Allah in ranks and in advancing columns, and go forth from their homes seeking My good pleasure, in the thousands. They purify their faces and their limbs, and gird their garments about their waists. Their sacrifice is their own blood, and their gospels are in their breasts. They are monks by night, lions by day. And I shall place among the people of his household and his descendants the foremost, the truthful, the martyrs, and the righteous. His community after him shall guide by truth and act with justice by it. I shall grant strength to whoever supports them, and aid whoever prays for them, and I shall bring the circle of evil down upon whoever opposes them or transgresses against them, or seeks to seize anything from what is in their hands. I shall make them heirs to their prophet and callers to their Lord, enjoining what is right and forbidding what is wrong, establishing prayer and giving alms, and fulfilling their covenant. I shall seal with them the goodness that I began with the first of them. That is My favor, which I grant to whom I will, and I am possessed of great favor.

This is how Ibn Abi Hatim related it, from Wahb ibn Munabbih al-Yamani, may Allah have mercy on him.

Then Ibn Abi Hatim said: My father told us, Abd al-Rahman ibn Salih told us, Abd al-Rahman ibn Muhammad ibn Ubaydullah al-Arzami told us, from Shayban al-Nahwi, Qatadah told me, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: When the verse was revealed: {O Prophet, indeed We have sent you as a witness, a bearer of good tidings, and a warner}, and he had already commanded Ali and Mu'adh to travel to Yemen, he said: Go forth, and give glad tidings, do not repel; make things easy, do not make them difficult, for indeed it has been revealed to me: {O Prophet, indeed We have sent you as a witness, a bearer of good tidings, and a warner}.

Al-Tabarani related it from Muhammad ibn Nasr ibn Humayd al-Bazzaz al-Baghdadi, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Salih al-Azdi, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Muhammad ibn Ubaydullah al-Arzami, with his chain, similarly. And he said at the end of it: "for indeed it has been revealed to me: O Prophet, indeed We have sent you as a witness over your community, a bearer of good tidings of Paradise, a warner against the Fire, one who calls to the testimony that there is no god but Allah by His permission, and a luminous lamp through the Qur'an."

His saying {a witness} means: a witness for Allah's oneness, that there is no god other than Him, and a witness over the people concerning their deeds on the Day of Resurrection, {and We have brought you as a witness over these}, like His saying {that you may be witnesses over mankind and that the Messenger may be a witness over you} [al-Baqarah: 143].

His saying {and a bearer of good tidings and a warner} means: a bearer of good tidings to the believers of abundant reward, and a warner to the disbelievers of grievous punishment.

His saying {and one who calls to Allah by His permission} means: one who calls creation to the worship of their Lord, by His command to you to do so. {and a luminous lamp} means: your affair is manifest in the truth you have brought, like the sun in its brightness and its illumination, which none denies except one who is obstinate.

His saying {and do not obey the disbelievers and the hypocrites, and disregard their harm} means: do not obey them, and do not listen to what they say. {and disregard their harm} means: overlook them and pass over them, and entrust their affair to Allah, for that is sufficient for dealing with them. That is why He said: {and rely upon Allah, and Allah is sufficient as a guardian}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ دَاوُدَ، حَدَّثَنَا فُلَيْح بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ هِلَالِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَارٍ قَالَ: لَقِيتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ فَقُلْتُ: أَخْبِرْنِي عَنْ صِفَةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي التَّوْرَاةِ. قَالَ: أَجَلْ، وَاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ لَمَوْصُوفٌ فِي التَّوْرَاةِ بِصِفَتِهِ فِي الْقُرْآنِ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ إِنَّا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ شَاهِدًا وَمُبَشِّرًا وَنَذِيرًا﴾ وَحِرْزًا لِلْأُمِّيِّينَ، أَنْتَ عَبْدِي وَرَسُولِي، سَمَّيْتُكَ الْمُتَوَكِّلَ، لَسْتَ بِفَظٍّ وَلَا غَلِيظٍ وَلَا سَخَّابٍ فِي الْأَسْوَاقِ، وَلَا يَدْفَعُ السَّيِّئَةَ بِالسَّيِّئَةِ، وَلَكِنْ يَعْفُو وَيَغْفِرُ ، وَلَنْ يقبضَه اللَّهُ حَتَّى يُقِيمَ بِهِ الْمِلَّةَ الْعَوْجَاءَ، بِأَنْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، فَيَفْتَحُ بِهَا أَعْيُنًا عُمْيًا، وَآذَانًا صُمًّا، وَقُلُوبًا غُلْفًا".

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ فِي "الْبُيُوعِ" عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سِنَانٍ، عَنْ فُلَيْح بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ هِلَالِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ بِهِ. وَرَوَاهُ فِي التَّفْسِيرِ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ -قِيلَ: ابْنِ رَجَاءٍ، وَقِيلَ: ابْنِ صَالِحٍ -عَنْ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ هِلَالٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَارٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، بِهِ . وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ رَجَاءٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ الْمَاجَشُونِ، بِهِ.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ فِي الْبُيُوعِ: وَقَالَ سَعِيدٌ، عَنْ هِلَالٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ سَلَامٍ.

وَقَالَ وَهْبُ بْنُ مُنَبِّهٍ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ أَوْحَى إِلَى نَبِيٌّ مِنْ أَنْبِيَاءِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ -يُقَالُ لَهُ: شَعْيَاءُ -أَنْ قُمْ فِي قَوْمِكَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَإِنِّي مَنْطِقٌ لِسَانَكَ بِوَحْيٍ وَأَبْعَثُ أُمِّيًّا مِنَ الْأُمِّيِّينَ، أَبْعَثُهُ [مُبَشِّرًا] لَيْسَ بِفَظٍّ وَلَا غَلِيظٍ وَلَا سَخَّابٍ فِي الْأَسْوَاقِ، لَوْ يَمُرُّ إِلَى جَنْبِ سِرَاجٍ لَمْ يُطْفِئْهُ، مِنْ سَكِينَتِهِ، وَلَوْ يَمْشِي عَلَى الْقَصَبِ لَمْ يُسْمَعْ مِنْ تَحْتِ قَدَمَيْهِ، أَبْعَثُهُ مُبَشِّرًا وَنَذِيرًا، لَا يَقُولُ الْخَنَا، أَفْتَحُ بِهِ أَعْيُنًا كُمْهًا ، وَآذَانًا صُمًّا، وَقُلُوبًا غُلْفًا، أسَدّده لِكُلِّ أَمْرٍ جَمِيلٍ، وَأَهَبُ لَهُ كُلَّ خُلُقٍ كَرِيمٍ، وَأَجْعَلُ السَّكِينَةَ لِبَاسَهُ، وَالْبِرَّ شِعَارَهُ، وَالتَّقْوَى ضَمِيرَهُ، وَالْحِكْمَةَ مَنْطِقَهُ، وَالصِّدْقَ وَالْوَفَاءَ طَبِيعَتَهُ، وَالْعَفْوَ وَالْمَعْرُوفَ خُلُقَهُ، وَالْحَقَّ شَرِيعَتَهُ، وَالْعَدْلَ سِيرَتَهُ، وَالْهُدَى إِمَامَهُ، وَالْإِسْلَامَ مِلَّتَهُ، وَأَحْمَدَ اسْمَهُ، أَهْدِي بِهِ بَعْدَ الضَّلَالَةِ، وَأُعَلِّمُ بِهِ بَعْدَ الْجَهَالَةِ، وَأَرْفَعُ بِهِ بَعْدَ الخَمَالة، وَأُعْرَفُ بِهِ بَعْدَ النُّكْرَة، وَأُكْثِّرُ بِهِ بَعْدَ الْقِلَّةِ، وَأُغْنِي بِهِ بَعْدَ العَيْلَة، وَأَجْمَعُ بِهِ بَعْدَ الْفُرْقَةِ، وَأُؤَلِّفُ بِهِ بَيْنَ أُمَمٍ مُتَفَرِّقَةٍ، وَقُلُوبٍ مُخْتَلِفَةٍ، وَأَهْوَاءٍ مُتَشَتَّتَةٍ، وَأَسْتَنْقِذُ بِهِ فِئامًا مِنَ النَّاسِ عَظِيمَةً مِنَ الْهَلَكَةِ، وَأَجْعَلُ أُمَّتَهُ خَيْرَ أُمَّةٍ أُخْرِجَتْ لِلنَّاسِ، يَأْمُرُونَ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَوْنَ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ، مُوَحِّدِينَ مُؤْمِنِينَ مُخْلِصِينَ، مُصَدِّقِينَ لِمَا جَاءَتْ بِهِ رُسُلِي ، أُلْهِمُهُمُ التَّسْبِيحَ وَالتَّحْمِيدَ، وَالثَّنَاءَ وَالتَّكْبِيرَ وَالتَّوْحِيدَ، فِي مَسَاجِدِهِمْ وَمَجَالِسِهِمْ، وَمَضَاجِعِهِمْ وَمُنْقَلَبِهِمْ وَمَثْوَاهُمْ، يُصَلُّونَ لِي قِيَامًا وَقُعُودًا، وَيُقَاتِلُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ صُفُوفًا وزُحوفا، وَيُخْرِجُونَ مِنْ دِيَارِهِمُ ابْتِغَاءَ مَرْضَاتِي أُلُوفًا، يُطَهِّرُونَ الْوُجُوهَ وَالْأَطْرَافَ، وَيَشُدُّونَ الثِّيَابَ فِي الْأَنْصَافِ، قُرْبَانُهُمْ دِمَاؤُهُمْ، وَأَنَاجِيلُهُمْ فِي صُدُورِهِمْ، رُهْبَانٌ بِاللَّيْلِ ليُوث بِالنَّهَارِ، وَأَجْعَلُ فِي أَهْلِ بَيْتِهِ وَذُرِّيَّتِهِ السَّابِقِينَ وَالصِّدِّيقِينَ وَالشُّهَدَاءَ وَالصَّالِحِينَ، أُمَّتُهُ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ يَهْدُونَ بِالْحَقِّ وَبِهِ يَعْدِلُونَ، أُعِزُّ مَنْ نَصَرَهُمْ، وَأُؤَيِّدُ مَنْ دَعَا لَهُمْ، وَأَجْعَلُ دَائِرَةَ السَّوْءِ عَلَى مَنْ خَالَفَهُمْ أَوْ بَغَى عَلَيْهِمْ، أَوْ أَرَادَ أَنْ يَنْتَزِعَ شَيْئًا مِمَّا فِي أَيْدِيهِمْ. أَجْعَلُهُمْ وَرَثَةً لِنَبِيِّهِمْ، وَالدَّاعِيَةَ إِلَى رَبِّهِمْ، يَأْمُرُونَ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَوْنَ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ، وَيُقِيمُونَ الصَّلَاةَ وَيُؤْتُونَ الزَّكَاةَ، وَيُوفُونَ بِعَهْدِهِمْ، أَخْتِمُ بِهِمُ الْخَيْرَ الَّذِي بَدَأْتُهُ بِأَوَّلِهِمْ، ذَلِكَ فَضْلِي أُوتِيهِ مَنْ أَشَاءُ، وَأَنَا ذُو الْفَضْلِ الْعَظِيمِ.

هَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، عَنْ وَهْبِ بْنِ مُنَبِّهٍ الْيَمَانِيِّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ صَالِحٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرحمن بن محمد بْنِ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ العَرْزَمي ، عَنْ شَيْبَان النَّحْوِيِّ، أَخْبَرَنِي قَتَادَةُ، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ إِنَّا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ شَاهِدًا وَمُبَشِّرًا وَنَذِيرًا﴾ -وَقَدْ كَانَ أَمَرَ عَلِيًّا وَمُعَاذًا أَنْ يَسِيرَا إِلَى الْيَمَنِ -فَقَالَ: "انْطَلِقَا فَبَشِّرَا وَلَا تُنَفِّرَا، وَيَسِّرَا وَلَا تُعَسِّرَا، إِنَّهُ قَدْ أُنْزِلَ عَلِيَّ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ إِنَّا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ شَاهِدًا وَمُبَشِّرًا وَنَذِيرًا﴾ .

وَرَوَاهُ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ نَصْرِ بْنِ حُمَيْدٍ الْبَزَّازِ الْبَغْدَادِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ صَالِحٍ الْأَزْدِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ [بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ] بْنِ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ الْعَرْزَمِيِّ، بِإِسْنَادِهِ مِثْلَهُ . وَقَالَ فِي آخِرِهِ: "فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ أُنْزِلَ عَلِيَّ: يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ إِنَّا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ شَاهِدًا عَلَى أُمَّتِكَ وَمُبَشِّرًا بِالْجَنَّةِ، وَنَذِيرًا مِنَ النَّارِ، وَدَاعِيًا إِلَى شَهَادَةِ أَنْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ بِإِذْنِهِ، وَسِرَاجًا مُنِيرًا بِالْقُرْآنِ".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿شَاهِدًا﴾ أَيْ: لِلَّهِ بِالْوَحْدَانِيَّةِ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ غَيْرُهُ، وَعَلَى النَّاسِ بِأَعْمَالِهِمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿وَجِئْنَا بِكَ عَلَى هَؤُلاءِ شَهِيدًا﴾ ، [كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿لِتَكُونُوا شُهَدَاءَ عَلَى النَّاسِ وَيَكُونَ الرَّسُولُ عَلَيْكُمْ شَهِيدًا﴾ ] [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٤٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمُبَشِّرًا وَنَذِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: بَشِيرًا لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِجَزِيلِ الثَّوَابِ، وَنَذِيرًا لِلْكَافِرِينَ مِنْ وَبِيلِ الْعِقَابِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَدَاعِيًا إِلَى اللَّهِ بِإِذْنِهِ﴾ أَيْ: دَاعِيًا لِلْخَلْقِ إِلَى عِبَادَةِ رَبِّهِمْ عَنْ أَمْرِهِ لَكَ بِذَلِكَ، ﴿وَسِرَاجًا مُنِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: وأمرُك ظَاهِرٌ فِيمَا جِئْتَ بِهِ مِنَ الْحَقِّ، كَالشَّمْسِ فِي إِشْرَاقِهَا وَإِضَاءَتِهَا، لَا يَجْحَدُهَا إِلَّا مُعَانِدٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا تُطِعِ الْكَافِرِينَ وَالْمُنَافِقِينَ وَدَعْ أَذَاهُمْ﴾ ، أَيْ: لَا تُطِعْهُمْ وَ [لَا] تَسْمَعْ مِنْهُمْ فِي الَّذِي يَقُولُونَهُ ﴿وَدَعْ أَذَاهُمْ﴾ أَيِ: اصْفَحْ وَتَجَاوَزْ عَنْهُمْ، وكِلْ أَمْرَهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ، فَإِنَّ فِيهِ كِفَايَةً لَهُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَتَوَكَّلْ عَلَى اللَّهِ وَكَفَى بِاللَّهِ وَكِيلا﴾ .

---

## 33:49 — verse 49

### Translation

This noble verse contains many rulings.

Among them: the application of the term "nikah" (marriage) to the contract alone. There is no verse in the Qur'an more explicit in this regard than this one. Scholars have differed concerning nikah: is it in reality applied to the contract alone, or to intercourse, or to both? There are three opinions on this. The usage of the Qur'an is generally applied to the contract together with the subsequent intercourse, except in this verse, where it is used for the contract alone, because of His saying: {If you marry believing women and then divorce them before you have touched them}. This verse also indicates the permissibility of divorcing a woman before consummating the marriage with her.

His saying, {believing women}, is stated according to the predominant case, since there is no difference in ruling, by consensus, between a believing woman and a woman of the People of the Book in this regard. Ibn Abbas, Sa'id ibn al-Musayyib, al-Hasan al-Basri, Ali ibn al-Husayn Zayn al-Abidin, and a group of the Salaf used this verse as evidence that divorce does not take effect unless it is preceded by a marriage, because Allah, Exalted is He, says: {If you marry believing women and then divorce them}, thus making the divorce follow the marriage, which indicates that divorce is not valid and does not take effect before it. This is the view of al-Shafi'i, Ahmad ibn Hanbal, and a large group of the Salaf and later scholars, may Allah have mercy on them all.

Malik and Abu Hanifah, may Allah have mercy on them both, held that divorce is valid before marriage, in the case where a man says: "If I marry so-and-so, she is divorced." According to them both, whenever he marries her she is divorced from him. They differed, however, regarding the case where a man says: "Every woman I marry is divorced." Malik said: she is not divorced until he specifies the particular woman. Abu Hanifah, may Allah have mercy on him, said: every woman he marries after this statement is divorced from him. The majority, however, argued against the occurrence of divorce in such cases by means of this verse.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas, who said: [If someone says]: "Every woman I marry is divorced," he said: this is of no effect, because Allah, Exalted is He, says: {O you who believe, if you marry believing women and then divorce them}, the verse.

He also narrated to us: [chain] from Ibn Abbas, who said: Allah, Exalted is He, only said: {If you marry believing women and then divorce them}. Do you not see that divorce comes after marriage?

Likewise, Muhammad ibn Ishaq narrated: [chain] from Ibn Abbas, who said: Allah said: {If you marry believing women and then divorce them}, so there is no divorce [before marriage].

A hadith to this effect has also come from Amr ibn Shu'ayb, from his father, from his grandfather, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "There is no divorce for the son of Adam concerning what he does not possess." Narrated by Imam Ahmad, al-Tirmidhi, Abu Dawud, and Ibn Majah. Al-Tirmidhi said: "This is a hasan (good) hadith," and it is the best thing that has been narrated on this subject. Likewise Ibn Majah narrated from Ali and al-Miswar ibn Makhramah, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "There is no divorce before marriage."

[In this verse there is evidence that the term "touching" (mass) is unrestricted, and that what is meant by it is intercourse.]

His saying, {so you have no waiting period ('iddah) that you may reckon against them}: this is a matter upon which the scholars are agreed, that a woman, if she is divorced before the marriage has been consummated with her, has no waiting period, so she may go and marry immediately whomever she wishes. The only exception to this is the woman whose husband has died, for she must observe a waiting period of four months and ten days from him, even if he had not consummated the marriage with her, by consensus as well.

His saying, {so provide for them and release them with a gracious release}: the mut'ah (provision/compensation given upon divorce) here is more general than being merely half of the specified dower, or the special mut'ah if no dower had been specified for her. Allah, Exalted is He, says: {And if you divorce them before you have touched them, and you have already specified for them a portion, then half of what you specified} [al-Baqarah: 237], and He says: {There is no blame upon you if you divorce women while you have not touched them nor specified for them a portion. But provide for them, upon the wealthy according to his capacity and upon the poor according to his capacity, a provision according to what is fair, an obligation upon those who do good} [al-Baqarah: 236].

In Sahih al-Bukhari, from Sahl ibn Sa'd and Abu Usayd: that the Messenger of Allah, peace and blessings of Allah be upon him, married Umaymah bint Sharahil, and when she was brought in to him he extended his hand toward her, and it seemed she disliked that, so he ordered Abu Usayd to provide for her and clothe her with two garments of Raziqi cloth.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with them both: if he had specified a dower for her, she is entitled to only half of it, and if he had not specified a dower for her, then let him provide for her according to his means, whether difficult or easy, and that is the gracious release.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ الْكَرِيمَةُ فِيهَا أَحْكَامٌ كَثِيرَةٌ. مِنْهَا: إِطْلَاقُ النِّكَاحِ عَلَى الْعَقْدِ وَحْدَهُ، وَلَيْسَ فِي الْقُرْآنِ آيَةٌ أَصْرَحُ فِي ذَلِكَ مِنْهَا، وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفُوا فِي النِّكَاحِ: هَلْ هُوَ حَقِيقَةً فِي الْعَقْدِ وَحْدَهُ، أَوْ فِي الْوَطْءِ، أَوْ فِيهِمَا؟ عَلَى ثَلَاثَةِ أَقْوَالِ، وَاسْتِعْمَالِ الْقُرْآنِ إِنَّمَا هُوَ فِي الْعَقْدِ وَالْوَطْءِ بَعْدَهُ، إِلَّا فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ فَإِنَّهُ اسْتُعْمِلَ فِي الْعَقْدِ وَحْدَهُ؛ لِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِذَا نَكَحْتُمُ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ ثُمَّ طَلَّقْتُمُوهُنَّ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ تَمَسُّوهُنَّ﴾ . وَفِيهَا دَلَالَةٌ لِإِبَاحَةِ طَلَاقِ الْمَرْأَةِ قَبْلَ الدُّخُولِ بها.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ﴾ خَرَجَ مَخْرَجَ الْغَالِبِ؛ إِذْ لَا فَرْقَ فِي الْحُكْمِ بَيْنَ الْمُؤْمِنَةِ وَالْكِتَابِيَّةِ فِي ذَلِكَ بِالِاتِّفَاقِ. وَقَدِ اسْتَدَلَّ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ المسَيَّب، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَعَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، زَيْنُ الْعَابِدِينَ، وَجَمَاعَةٌ مِنَ السَّلَفِ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ عَلَى أَنَّ الطَّلَاقَ لَا يَقَعُ إِلَّا إِذَا تَقَدَّمَهُ نِكَاحٌ؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى قَالَ: ﴿إِذَا نَكَحْتُمُ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ ثُمَّ طَلَّقْتُمُوهُنَّ﴾ ، فَعَقَّبَ النِّكَاحَ بِالطَّلَاقِ، فَدَلَّ عَلَى أَنَّهُ لَا يَصِحُّ وَلَا يَقَعُ قَبْلَهُ. وَهَذَا مَذْهَبُ الشَّافِعِيِّ، وَأَحْمَدَ بْنِ حَنْبَلٍ، وَطَائِفَةٍ كَثِيرَةٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ، رَحِمَهُمُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى.

وَذَهَبَ مَالِكٌ وَأَبُو حَنِيفَةَ، رَحِمَهُمَا اللَّهُ، إِلَى صِحَّةِ الطَّلَاقِ قَبْلَ النِّكَاحِ؛ فِيمَا إِذَا قَالَ: "إِنْ تَزَوَّجْتُ فُلَانَةً فَهِيَ طَالِقٌ". فَعِنْدَهُمَا مَتَى تَزَوَّجَهَا طُلِّقَتْ مِنْهُ. وَاخْتَلَفَا فِيمَا إِذَا قَالَ: "كُلُّ امْرَأَةٍ أَتَزَوَّجُهَا فَهِيَ طَالِقٌ". فَقَالَ مَالِكٌ: لَا تُطَلَّقُ حَتَّى يُعَيِّنَ الْمَرْأَةَ. وَقَالَ أَبُو حَنِيفَةَ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: كُلُّ امْرَأَةٍ يَتَزَوَّجُهَا بَعْدَ هَذَا الْكَلَامِ تُطَلَّقُ مِنْهُ، فَأَمَّا الْجُمْهُورُ فَاحْتَجُّوا عَلَى عَدَمِ وُقُوعِ الطَّلَاقِ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ الْمَرْوَزِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا النَّضْرُ بْنُ شُمَيْل، حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ -سَمِعْتُ آدَمَ مَوْلَى خَالِدٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: [إِذَا قَالَ] : كُلُّ امْرَأَةٍ أَتَزَوَّجُهَا فَهِيَ طَالِقٌ، قَالَ: لَيْسَ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ أَجْلِ أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِذَا نَكَحْتُمُ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ ثُمَّ طَلَّقْتُمُوهُنَّ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَحَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ الأحْمَسِي، حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، عَنْ مَطَرٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ مُسْلِمِ بْنِ يَنّاق ، عَنْ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: إِنَّمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِذَا نَكَحْتُمُ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ ثُمَّ طَلَّقْتُمُوهُنَّ﴾ ، أَلَا تَرَى أَنَّ الطَّلَاقَ بَعْدَ النِّكَاحِ؟!

وَهَكَذَا رَوَى مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ دَاوُدَ بْنِ الْحُصَيْنِ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿إِذَا نَكَحْتُمُ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ ثُمَّ طَلَّقْتُمُوهُنَّ﴾ فَلَا طَلَاقَ [قَبْلَ النِّكَاحِ] .

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ الْحَدِيثُ بِذَلِكَ عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ شُعَيْبٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا طَلَاقَ لِابْنِ آدَمَ فِيمَا لَا يَمْلِكُ". رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ . وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: "هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ". وَهُوَ أَحْسَنُ شَيْءٍ رُوِيَ فِي هَذَا الْبَابِ. وَهَكَذَا رَوَى ابْنُ مَاجَهْ عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، والمِسْوَر بْنِ مَخْرَمَة عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "لَا طَلَاقَ قَبْلَ نِكَاحٍ" .

[وَفِي الْآيَةِ دَلِيلٌ عَلَى أَنَّ الْمَسِيسَ مُطْلَقٌ، وَيُرَادُ بِهِ الْوَطْءُ] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ : ﴿فَمَا لَكُمْ عَلَيْهِنَّ مِنْ عِدَّةٍ تَعْتَدُّونَهَا﴾ : هَذَا أَمْرٌ مُجْمَعٌ عَلَيْهِ بَيْنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ: أَنَّ الْمَرْأَةَ إِذَا طُلِّقَتْ قَبْلَ الدُّخُولِ بِهَا لَا عِدَّةَ عَلَيْهَا فَتَذْهَبُ فَتَتَزَوَّجُ فِي فَوْرِهَا مَنْ شَاءَتْ، وَلَا يُسْتَثْنَى مِنْ هَذَا إِلَّا الْمُتَوَفَّى عَنْهَا زَوْجُهَا، فَإِنَّهَا تَعْتَدُّ مِنْهُ أَرْبَعَةَ أَشْهُرٍ وَعَشْرًا، وَإِنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ دَخَلَ بِهَا بِالْإِجْمَاعِ أَيْضًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَمَتِّعُوهُنَّ وَسَرِّحُوهُنَّ سَرَاحًا جَمِيلا﴾ : الْمُتْعَةُ هَاهُنَا أَعَمُّ مِنْ أَنْ تَكُونَ نِصْفَ الصَّدَاقِ الْمُسَمَّى، أَوِ الْمُتْعَةُ الْخَاصَّةُ إِنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ قَدْ سَمَّى لَهَا، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ طَلَّقْتُمُوهُنَّ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ تَمَسُّوهُنَّ وَقَدْ فَرَضْتُمْ لَهُنَّ فَرِيضَةً فَنِصْفُ مَا فَرَضْتُمْ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٣٧] ، وَقَالَ ﴿لَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْكُمْ إِنْ طَلَّقْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ مَا لَمْ تَمَسُّوهُنَّ أَوْ تَفْرِضُوا لَهُنَّ فَرِيضَةً وَمَتِّعُوهُنَّ عَلَى الْمُوسِعِ قَدَرُهُ وَعَلَى الْمُقْتِرِ قَدَرُهُ مَتَاعًا بِالْمَعْرُوفِ حَقًّا عَلَى الْمُحْسِنِينَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٣٦] .

وَفِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، عَنْ سَهْلِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ وَأَبِي أُسَيْدٍ؛ أن رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم تَزَوَّجَ أُمَيْمَةَ بِنْتَ شَرَاحيل، فَلَمَّا أُدْخِلَتْ عَلَيْهِ بَسَطَ يَدَهُ إِلَيْهَا، فَكَأَنَّهَا كَرِهَتْ ذَلِكَ، فَأَمَرَ أَبَا أَسِيدٍ أَنْ يُجَهِّزَهَا وَيَكْسُوَهَا ثَوْبَيْنِ رازقيَّين .

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا: إِنْ كَانَ سَمَّى لَهَا صَدَاقًا، فَلَيْسَ لَهَا إِلَّا النِّصْفُ، وَإِنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ سَمَّى لَهَا صَدَاقًا فَأَمْتِعَهَا عَلَى قَدْرِ عُسْرِهِ وَيُسْرِهِ، وَهُوَ السَّرَاحُ الْجَمِيلُ.

---

## 33:50 — verse 50

### Translation

The Almighty is speaking, addressing His Prophet, the prayers and peace of Allah be upon him, telling him that He has made lawful for him from among women his wives to whom he gave their bridal payments, which are the "wages" (ujur) mentioned here, as Mujahid and more than one other have said. The Prophet's ﷺ bridal payment for his wives was twelve uqiyyahs and a nashsh, which is half an uqiyyah, the total being five hundred dirhams, except for Umm Habibah bint Abi Sufyan, for whom the Negus, may Allah have mercy on him, paid on his behalf a bridal payment of four hundred dinars, and except for Safiyyah bint Huyayy, whom he selected from among the captives of Khaybar, then freed her and made her freedom her bridal payment. Likewise Juwayriyyah bint al-Harith al-Mustaliqiyyah: he paid off her ransom (kitabah) to Thabit ibn Qays ibn Shammas and married her. May Allah be pleased with all of them.

Regarding His saying, {and whoever your right hand possesses from what Allah has granted you as spoils}: that is, He permitted you to take concubines (tasarri) from what you took of the war spoils. He possessed Safiyyah and Juwayriyyah, then freed them and married them. He also possessed Rayhanah bint Sham'un al-Nadriyyah, and Mariyah the Copt, the mother of his son Ibrahim (peace be upon him), and these two were among the concubines (sarari). May Allah be pleased with them.

Regarding His saying, {and the daughters of your paternal uncle, and the daughters of your paternal aunts, and the daughters of your maternal uncle, and the daughters of your maternal aunts, who emigrated with you}: this is a just balance between excess and deficiency.
